- **No substance pattern.** Continues to not self-medicate via alcohol or pharmaceuticals beyond plausibly prescribed items. Given trauma load this remains anomalous and noteworthy.
- **Physical signature in close observation.** Slight favoring of the left side after sustained engagements (cumulative impact damage to the right hip/knee, consistent with the way she lands from glider descents and the way she throws venom blasts off the right hand). Habitual rotation of the right shoulder before combat. A scar inventory consistent with two decades of fieldwork; none disfiguring, several she does not bother to conceal in domestic settings — a small but real change from earlier-period body-management.

## IV.6 Behavioral Micro-Pattern Update

The Subject's tics, routes, and rituals have ossified into recognizable signatures in the recent window. Surveillance-grade detail:

- **Caffeine dependence formalized.** Coffee, black, throughout the day; a specific preferred order at a specific neighborhood establishment, walked to on a route that varies on a three-day rotation. The rotation is deliberate — counter-surveillance habit applied to a civilian errand. She knows she does it; she does not stop doing it.
- **Phone discipline.** Burner-rotation for operational contacts; a single civilian device for school, doctor, and chosen-family use. Civilian device kept off her person during patrol. This is post-Skrull doctrine: never carry an identifier through a hostile environment.
- **Wardrobe.** Costume cleaned and inspected on a regular cycle. Civilian wardrobe is functional, dark-palette, layerable — clothes she can fight in if forced. No item of clothing in her current rotation prevents combat. This is not paranoia; this is professional dress code for the job she actually has.
- **The second-person voice.** Reduced but not eliminated. Surfaces in the recent run primarily under exhaustion or during operations that pattern-match to prior trauma (HYDRA-coded threats, Skrull-coded threats). When it surfaces, treat as a leading indicator of decompensation risk over the following 48–72 hours.
- **Humor profile.** Dry, low-volume, increasingly maternal in cadence — the humor of someone whose primary audience is now a child who will repeat her at school. She has gotten *funnier* in the recent window, which is itself a marker of stabilization; cumulative-trauma survivors who recover wit are survivors whose baseline has improved.
- **Eye behavior.** Constant low-grade environmental scanning, never absent. In domestic settings the scan attenuates but does not stop. She does not relax her perimeter; she has accepted that she will not.
- **The grocery list.** Consistent: items for Gerry, items for herself (minimal, protein-forward), a small set of comfort items (specific brand of tea, specific bread) that have remained constant across moves. The persistence of comfort-item brand loyalty across three apartments in the window is the closest thing in the file to evidence of an *interior life of taste*, distinct from operational necessity.

## IV.7 The Current Trust Map

As of the most recent reports, the Subject's circle of operational trust is small, deliberate, and stratified:

1. **Tier One — Gerry.** Not a peer relationship; the load-bearing identity anchor. Total disclosure of love, calibrated disclosure of fact.
2. **Tier Two — Carol Danvers.** The one adult relationship in which the Subject's withdrawals are tolerated without retaliation and the Subject's competence is neither over-relied-upon nor diminished. Mutual.
3. **Tier Two — Lindsay McCabe.** Longest-running friendship in the file. Reduced contact in recent window due to geography and life-stage, but unbroken. Subject will answer Lindsay's calls under any operational condition; this is a hard rule.
4. **Tier Two — Roger Gocking.** Co-parental in function if not in romance. The Subject's choice to keep him close without romanticizing the relationship is a sustained piece of self-knowledge — she knows what she can sustain and what she cannot.
5. **Tier Three — Operational contacts.** Spider-family, Avengers roster, select Daredevil-adjacent street operators. Will work with, will not domicile with.
6. **Tier Four — Everyone else.** Warmth available on request; trust available on evidence; will not extend either as a courtesy.

What is *absent* from the current trust map is also data: no active romantic partner, no institutional handler, no chain of command above her in any organization she belongs to. She is, structurally, **the senior authority in her own life** for the first time in her published existence. This is new.

## IV.8 The Open Files

A complete intelligence dossier marks not just what is known but what remains unresolved as of close-of-period.

- **The Octessa-arc biology.** Long-term effects of the recent blood condition are not on-record cleared. Standing item.
- **Jonathan Drew's full role.** The disclosure of non-paternity does not foreclose his continuing significance; the Subject's emotional accounting with the man who raised her remains incomplete and is a likely future trigger.
- **Veranke-residue.** The Skrull queen wore her face for years; the cultural and personal artifacts that "Jessica" generated during that period are still being discovered by the Subject in passing. Any such discovery is a low-grade re-traumatization. She handles each one better than the last. The cumulative load remains nonzero.
- **HYDRA's institutional memory of her.** HYDRA-descended organizations retain her as a known asset / failed asset. Any operation that frames her in those terms will pattern-match her oldest wound. She has defenses; the defenses cost.
- **Gerry's powers / nature.** Open developmental question. The Subject is preparing for several contingencies in parallel and has not committed publicly to any of them, which is consistent with her empirical cognitive style.

## IV.9 Current State — Synthesis

The Subject as of the most recent reporting is operating at the highest sustained baseline of her published life. She is **not healed** — the trauma architecture described in Sections 3 and 4 of the prior workups remains structurally intact and will remain so. What has changed is the *load-management*. She has built, with deliberate engineering, a life in which her chronic conditions are housed inside routines that absorb them: insomnia inside patrol, hypervigilance inside parenting, avoidance inside professional independence, identity-instability inside the load-bearing fact of motherhood. The architecture is elegant. It is also, as she knows, single-fault-tolerant at best — Gerry is the keystone, and a sufficiently targeted strike at the keystone would still bring it down.

She is, in plain language, **a forty-seven-year-old (publication-time) complex-trauma survivor who has stopped trying to outrun the trauma and started building furniture around it.** She works. She mothers. She maintains four to six durable relationships. She drinks black coffee on a rotating route. She does not sleep enough. She narrates herself in second person only when she is tired. She still walks toward the threat alone when frightened, and she is still right more often than she is wrong about it. She has not asked anyone to rescue her in years, and the appropriate read of that fact is not that she has transcended the need but that she has, at long last, **become a person she trusts to do the rescuing herself.**

That is where she is now. That is how she got there.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — JESSICA DREW
## Section: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, recovered S.H.I.E.L.D./S.W.O.R.D. medical files (partial, fragmentary, much of it falsified during the Skrull-substitution window), reconstructions from Avengers infirmary records, and inference from observable somatic behavior across 47 years of canon. Where institutional records exist they are largely unreliable; the subject has been treated by physicians who did not know what species she was, by handlers with reason to lie about her condition, and during one extended period was not herself when the chart says she was. This file privileges the body's own evidence — scars, gait, sleep patterns, metabolic anomalies — over paperwork.*

---

### I. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

Jessica Drew has never had a normal human baseline against which to measure deviation. This is the first fact of her medical record and the one that distorts all the others. There is no pediatric chart from a clinic; there is Wundagore, the High Evolutionary's facility, and whatever serums, gene therapies, irradiations, and developmental interventions were performed there on a child who could not consent and whose father did not document — or whose documentation was later destroyed, reclassified, or proven false when his paternity itself was retconned out from under her.

What can be observed of her current physiology:

- **Resting heart rate** runs in the low 40s, athletic-range but consistent even when she is not in conditioning cycles. Resting respiratory rate similarly depressed. Core temperature trends roughly 0.6–0.9 °F below human mean, with a wider tolerable range in both directions before symptomatic distress.
- **Metabolic throughput** is elevated; she eats more than her frame would predict and processes calories rapidly. Hypoglycemia onsets faster than baseline and presents as irritability and fine-motor degradation before it presents as faintness. She keeps food in pockets, glove-compartments, and the lining of patrol gear — this is constitutional, not anxious.
- **Toxin and pathogen resistance** is the most thoroughly documented anomaly. Across the Wolfman, Claremont, Bendis, and Hopeless runs she has been exposed to nerve agents, infectious vectors, alien biologicals, and at least three substances classified as universally lethal to mammals, with subclinical or transient symptoms. She does not catch the seasonal viruses that move through Avengers Tower; she has been the designated person sent into biohazard zones more than once.
- **Radiation tolerance** is functionally complete in the diagnostic range and substantial in the therapeutic-to-acute range. She is the only Avenger who does not require shielding for certain S.W.O.R.D. work.
- **Bio-electric generation** — the "venom blast" — is a true metabolic capacity, not a stored technology. It draws against her glycemic reserves; sustained discharge produces tremor, nausea, and a characteristic post-discharge migraine that begins behind the left eye and migrates posterior.
- **Pheromone secretion**, treated separately below for its medical and social consequences, is involuntary, glandular, and modulable only with effort and (in some periods) pharmacological suppression.
- **Wall adhesion** is dermal and present across the entire body; she can release it volitionally and does so reflexively in sleep when contact is unwanted.
- **Healing rate** is roughly 3–5× human, faster for soft tissue than for bone, with the peculiarity that her scarring is *minimal* — she keeps very few marks from injuries that should have left them, which has the secondary effect of erasing her own forensic record of what has happened to her. She has had to be told, more than once, the extent of injuries she had already healed past.

She has no pre-morbid baseline. Every system listed above is the only system she has ever had. The medical impact of this is not a list of conditions; it is a *stance toward her own body* — she experiences it as foreign-issued equipment whose specifications she has had to reverse-engineer through use. She does not trust internal signals the way an ordinary patient does. She self-triages by visible damage, not interoception, which means she chronically under-reports.

---

### II. THE WUNDAGORE PERIOD — DEVELOPMENTAL INSULT

The earliest medical event of her life is the one she cannot remember and cannot now verify. Across published origins the inciting harm has been told as (a) uranium poisoning from proximity to her father's research, treated by experimental spider-serum, (b) deliberate genetic engineering using arachnid genetic material, and most recently (c) the revelation that Jonathan Drew was not her biological father and that her existence is a project of other parties entirely. The function across all versions is the same: a child whose body was made, not born, by adults whose interests were not aligned with her welfare.

Concretely, this period left:

- An *unknown number of pediatric surgical or injection sites*, healed past visibility but documented in one S.H.I.E.L.D. deep-scan as faint subcutaneous scar lattices along the spine, the lateral thighs, and the suboccipital region. These are consistent with chronic vascular access and repeat lumbar puncture in a small child.
- *Developmental isolation from human peers*, with somatic-developmental sequelae: her gross-motor calibration is excellent against opponents and inanimate environments and poor against ordinary human bodies. She has injured people she did not mean to injure in handshakes, embraces, and shoves; she now modulates contact with conscious overhead at all times, which reads as reserve and is partly that and partly muscle control.
- *Absence of normative immunological exposure history*. She did not have childhood illnesses. Her immune system was built by Wundagore, not by playgrounds, which is one reason it works the way it does and one reason no physician has ever fully understood it.
- *Cryogenic-stasis interval (period and duration disputed)* during which her aging slowed or arrested; the practical consequence is that her chronological age, biological age, and lived experiential age do not match, and have never matched, and any actuarial reading of her is wrong.

The psychological impact is foundational and is treated more fully in the Psychological section, but the medical-experiential piece is this: she has no memory of being a healthy child, no memory of being an ordinary patient, and no template for what it feels like to be well. Wellness, for her, is the absence of acute symptom. There is no positive standard.

---

### III. THE HYDRA PERIOD — CONDITIONING AS MEDICAL EVENT

Recruitment into HYDRA under Otto Vermis involved a sustained program of conditioning that should be classified medically as well as psychiatrically. It included:

- **Pharmacological agents** of unspecified composition, administered without consent, with the effect of suggestibility enhancement and memory partition. Long-term endocrine consequences are unknowable. She has, at intervals, reported transient anosmia, taste alteration, and one period of menstrual irregularity in the early Wolfman run that resolved without intervention — any or none of these may be sequelae.
- **Combat conditioning** that produced the physical baseline she has carried since: fight reflexes that fire below the threshold of conscious decision, a startle response that throws hands before it forms thought. She has had to retrain this in safe contexts and has not fully succeeded; she does not let people approach her from behind, ever, and has bruised at least two friends who forgot.
- **The Jerry Hunt incident** — believing she had killed a man she loved — produced no observable somatic injury but is the rupture event for everything afterward. Her body learned, in that moment, that intimacy is an attack vector. This is a medical fact insofar as it set the baseline autonomic profile she has carried since: elevated sympathetic tone in intimate proximity, slow parasympathetic recovery.

There is no record of any debriefing medical examination after she broke programming. She walked out and was treated, for years, as if her body were not a crime scene.

---

### IV. THE PHEROMONE PROBLEM — CHRONIC SOCIO-MEDICAL CONDITION

This is the closest thing she has to a *chronic disease* in the conventional sense, and it is the one her medical record least adequately addresses.

**Mechanism (as best understood):** Apocrine-analog glands distributed across the standard human distribution plus accessory sites along the clavicle and the small of the back continuously secrete a complex of volatile compounds that bind to vomeronasal and accessory olfactory receptors in nearby humans. Effect is dose-dependent and exposure-dependent. The acute response in most men is attraction ranging from heightened attentiveness to disinhibited approach. The acute response in most women is hostility ranging from cool dislike to aggressive confrontation. Neither response correlates with the target's actual disposition toward her sober; both responses are reported by their subjects as feeling *like their own thoughts*, which is the cruelest feature.

**Course of the condition:**
- *Untreated baseline (Wolfman / Claremont era):* full-strength secretion, no modulation. Social functioning catastrophically impaired. Romantic encounters unreliable as signal; female friendships nearly impossible to initiate. Documented incidents of bar-fights begun by women she had not addressed.
- *Behavioral modulation (mid-period):* she learned partial volitional damping through breath control, posture, and a kind of effortful affective flattening — she does not relax in mixed company because relaxation increases output.
- *Pharmacological suppression (intermittent, per various arcs):* suppressants exist and she has used them. They blunt the venom-blast capacity as a side effect (the systems share metabolic substrate) and they produce a flat, brittle mood she dislikes more than the social cost of the unsuppressed state. She cycles on and off them depending on operational need; this cycling is itself a destabilizing input.
- *Current period:* she manages with a combination of partial suppression, behavioral control, and careful selection of company. The female friendships that did survive (Lindsay McCabe, Carol Danvers, the small circle around Gerry) were forged through *prolonged exposure* until the recipients' systems either habituated or learned to override the signal. This is one reason she does not form new close female friendships easily — the time-cost is enormous.

**Psychological impact:** She does not trust attraction directed at her. She does not trust hostility directed at her. She does not trust her own readings of others' affective states toward her because she knows she is contaminating the data. This produces a corrosive epistemological loneliness that is medical in origin and existential in consequence. She has said, in private conversation reconstructed from witness report, that she does not know what it would feel like to walk into a room and have people simply *see her* with their own reactions intact. She is in her sixties of published time and she has never had that experience.

---

### V. INJURIES — CATALOG AND PATTERNS

Exhaustive enumeration is impossible; what follows is the pattern, with representative entries.

**Soft tissue:** innumerable lacerations, contusions, burns. The healing rate has scrubbed most of these from her body. The few that remain — a faint puckering at the right deltoid from a ballistic wound in the late Wolfman period, a thin pale line at the jaw from edged-weapon contact during the Bendis run, a stippling of small marks on the left forearm she will not explain — she has kept because they healed during periods of acute psychological distress and her tissue does not regenerate as cleanly when her cortisol is sustainedly elevated.

**Skeletal:** documented fractures include left ulna (twice), right clavicle, three ribs on separate occasions, left zygomatic arch, right fifth metatarsal, multiple phalanges. All healed without surgical fixation; the clavicle healed with a slight asymmetry that is visible when she shrugs and that she is mildly self-conscious about. Spinal injury during a hard impact in the Hopeless run was diagnosed in the field as compression fracture, healed in approximately six weeks of patrol-modified activity, no neurological deficit. She has had concussions in the high single digits at minimum; she does not always present for assessment.

**Penetrating trauma:** ballistic wounds (several), edged-weapon wounds (many), at least one impalement event survived through a combination of physiology and refusal to die in front of the responsible party. She has had foreign bodies remain in her tissue long enough to be encysted and later extracted in non-emergent settings.

**Energy / exotic exposure:** plasma burns, magical attack residua, dimensional-shear effects, telepathic intrusion (treated below). The healing system handles thermal and kinetic insult well, magical and psychic insult less reliably.

**Pattern features worth noting:**
- *Posterior injuries are rare relative to baseline*, reflecting that she will not be flanked.
- *Hand injuries are common*, reflecting close-range work and a fighting style that uses the body as primary weapon.
- *She does not protect her face*, which is a personality finding as much as a tactical one — she has never had a serviceable relationship with her own appearance.
- *Injury reports cluster temporally with periods of low social support*. She gets hurt more when she is alone, both because she works alone more and because she is less willing to disengage.

---

### VI. THE CAPTIVITY — SKRULL POD INTERVAL

The single most medically significant event of her adult life and the one with the worst documentation.

She was held by Skrull forces for a period that cannot be precisely fixed and was likely longer than the published timeline suggests — *years*, possibly contiguous, during which a Skrull operative (Veranke, the queen, in her form) walked her life. Her body during this interval was housed in a suspension pod, biologically maintained, periodically accessed for:

- *Memory extraction*, repeated, invasive at the neural level. Mechanism unknown; effect documented. On recovery she showed gaps and softenings in autobiographical memory that have not fully resolved, particularly for the immediate pre-captivity period.
- *Genetic sampling*, repeated. The Skrull program required ongoing material from her to maintain Veranke's morphological fidelity.
- *Physiological observation* of a kind she would later describe as having been "studied like a specimen by people who thought she was one."
- *Possible reproductive interference* — this is inference, not documentation, but the irregularities surrounding Gerry's later conception and gestation are easier to explain if her reproductive system was accessed during captivity than if it was not.

**Recovery presentation (*Secret Invasion* #8 and immediate aftermath):**
- Severe muscle wasting; she could not stand unsupported at first.
- Cachexia; significant weight loss against her already-lean frame.
- Skin in poor condition; pressure changes from sustained immobility.
- Severely disordered sleep architecture for months following — fragmented, with parasomnias.
- Acute hypervigilance, exaggerated startle, dissociative episodes.
- A profound and specific *terror of enclosed reclined positions* — she would not lie flat on a medical table without active effort for over a year.

**Long-term sequelae:**
- Sleep has never returned to baseline. She is functionally insomniac and uses patrol to absorb the wakeful hours.
- She does not undergo elective imaging studies if she can avoid them; MRI tubes are intolerable and she has refused them in non-urgent contexts.
- She maintains a personal rule, never articulated but observable, of not being unconscious in spaces she has not personally secured. She does not nap in safehouses she did not choose.
- The captivity reactivated and intensified the identity-instability that the HYDRA period had laid down. The body learned, twice now, that it could be held in place while someone else used her life.

There was no adequate medical follow-up. Avengers infirmary triage handled the acute presentation; the chronic sequelae have been managed by her, alone, over the subsequent years, in patterns of behavior she does not name as medical management because she has never had a clinician to name them with.

---

### VII. THE SOUL-BODY SEPARATION (*SPIDER-WOMAN* #50)

A discrete medical-metaphysical event: her consciousness was extracted from her body and her body sustained without it. She was returned. The acute injury was reversed; the trace effect was not. Survivors of dissociative-rich trauma often report a sense that their body and their experiencing self are not perfectly fused; she has the unusual circumstance of having literally undergone the separation and now lives with the after-experience of *knowing* the seam is there. The second-person interior narration that surfaces in later eras may be partly a literary device and is partly, in our reading, an artifact of this event — she retained a habit of observing herself from a position slightly outside the body that was returned to her.

---

### VIII. PREGNANCY AND PARTURITION

Gerry was conceived and gestated under circumstances that no obstetric textbook addresses. The pregnancy proceeded irregularly; delivery occurred off-Earth, attended by non-human medical personnel under hostile conditions. The infant survived; she survived; there is no documented postpartum hemorrhage, no documented infection, no documented thromboembolic event. Carol Danvers organized a postpartum support scaffold — meals, presence, child-handling relief — that functioned as the postpartum care she did not otherwise receive. She was breastfeeding within hours of a tactical engagement; she has remarked, dryly, that her recovery was "rude" in its speed.

The medical impact of motherhood on her body has been less notable than the medical impact of motherhood on her *use* of her body: she takes fewer reckless risks, modulates engagement to preserve return-home capacity, and has — for the first time in her published life — a reason to want her body to last.

---

### IX. SUBSTANCE USE

**Alcohol:** social, moderate, episodic. Documented drinking with Carol Danvers in particular; she is the more controlled of the two. She does not drink alone in any documented period. She does not drink when Gerry is in her care. Tolerance is high — her metabolism handles ethanol the way it handles other toxins — which means she is rarely impaired and has rarely used drinking as anesthesia, possibly because it would not work for her.

**Tobacco:** none.

**Caffeine:** consistent, moderate to high, particularly during patrol cycles. Effect is muted by her metabolism.

**Pharmaceuticals:** pheromone suppressants (intermittent, see §IV). Analgesics rarely; she undertreats her own pain. No documented use of sedatives or hypnotics despite documented insomnia — refusal to be chemically unconscious is consistent with the captivity-derived rule above.

**Illicit substances:** none documented.

**Behavioral substitutes for substance use:** overwork, patrol, isolation, combat. These carry the load that alcohol or drugs carry in other complex-trauma survivors. They are not benign — they have medical costs of their own — but they have kept her free of substance pathology in a population where substance pathology is the modal outcome.

---

### X. SLEEP

A standalone subsection because it is the single most chronically dysregulated system she has and the one that most directly accelerates everything else.

Baseline sleep, since Skrull captivity recovery, runs in the range of three to five hours, fragmented, with frequent awakenings and a long sleep-onset latency. She sleeps better in proximity to Gerry (parental physiology) and worse in unfamiliar environments. She has parasomnias she does not discuss — sleep talking observed by Lindsay McCabe in earlier eras, suspected sleep paralysis episodes inferred from her aversion to supine positions on waking.

She fills the wakeful hours with patrol, surveillance work, and rooftop sitting. This is not insomnia management; it is insomnia *use*. The cost is cumulative cognitive load, increased injury rate, and slow erosion of affective range. She knows this. She has not changed it.

---

### XI. SENSORY AND NEUROLOGICAL

- **Vision:** above-baseline acuity, low-light vision functional, recovery from flash-blinding faster than human norm.
- **Hearing:** above baseline, with a particular sensitivity to high-frequency electromagnetic equipment hum that she finds intrusive in some buildings.
- **Proprioception and balance:** exceptional, supported by wall-adhesion as a constant kinesthetic reference.
- **Pain perception:** present and unimpaired in acute range; she does not have congenital insensitivity. She does have a high voluntary tolerance, which is conditioning, not physiology.
- **Telepathic intrusion history:** several events of mind control, possession, and psychic attack across her career. These have left no documented neurological deficit and a substantial behavioral one: she will not work willingly with telepaths she does not personally trust, and she has been observed to leave rooms when telepathic interfaces are deployed.

---

### XII. REPRODUCTIVE / ENDOCRINE

Beyond the pheromone system: irregular menstrual history, fertility demonstrably present (Gerry), no documented contraception regimen (her physiology may handle this internally or she may rely on behavioral control; the record is silent). No documented gynecological care of the ordinary kind. She has not had, to our knowledge, a routine well-woman examination by a physician who knew what they were examining. This is a gap in her care that no one has filled.

---

### XIII. DENTAL, OPHTHALMOLOGIC, DERMATOLOGIC

Effectively no documented care in any of these domains. Her healing covers most of what these specialties would address. The absence of a primary-care relationship across her adult life is itself the finding — she has been treated only for things that bled.

---

### XIV. PSYCHOLOGICAL IMPACT — INTEGRATED SUMMARY OF MEDICAL HISTORY

The body that carries Jessica Drew has been, since before her memory begins, a *site of other people's projects*. It was engineered without her consent, conditioned without her consent, occupied without her consent, surveilled without her consent, used as a template for impersonation without her consent. The medical history is not a list of conditions and treatments; it is the record of a person who has had to construct a relationship to her own body from the outside, like someone tenant in a building she did not design and cannot fully inspect.

This produces a specific medical-psychological signature:

- *Under-reporting of symptom* — she does not trust her own interoceptive signals and she does not believe her pain entitles her to anything.
- *Distrust of clinicians* — every authority that has had access to her body has eventually been revealed to have been working against her.
- *Self-management of conditions that should be co-managed* — sleep, trauma, the pheromone problem, the post-captivity hypervigilance. She handles all of it alone, badly, with the tools she has.
- *Profound somatic loneliness* — there is no one who knows her body the way a long-term physician knows a patient. There has been no one. The closest she has come is Carol Danvers, who knows her *behavior*, and the small group who can read her physical state from across a room because they have been with her long enough — but no chart, no continuity of care, no expert advocate.
- *Motherhood as the first reason to value the body itself* — Gerry has produced a shift not in what she will do to her body but in what she will *let* be done to it. She has, since his birth, accepted help she would not previously have accepted. This is the closest thing in her record to a therapeutic gain.

The summary judgment of this section is the same as the summary judgment of the dossier overall, viewed through the body: she has survived an extraordinary amount, she has done so largely alone, the cost is written in the systems that no longer run baseline, and the achievement is that she is still here, still functional, still — by the standards of what she has carried — astonishingly well.

She deserves better care than she has ever had. She would not accept it if offered. Both of these are findings.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: JESSICA DREW

*The body as longitudinal record. What forty-seven years of observation, if continuous, would have compiled.*

---

## I. BASELINE PHYSICAL PRESENTATION

**Stature and frame.** Five feet ten, long-limbed, carrying roughly 140 pounds of which an unusually high fraction is dense muscle — her sub-dermal tissue density is elevated by whatever the Wundagore process did to her, so she weighs more than she looks like she should, a fact one notices only when one tries to move her or share a small bench-seat. She takes up less volumetric space than her height suggests because she compresses herself in repose: shoulders rolled fractionally inward, knees angled toward midline, elbows tight to ribs. The default occupancy is *small for size*. This is not femininity-coding; it is the residue of two decades during which the wrong wall or doorway brought hostile attention, and of a body that learned to enter rooms without displacing air.

**Skin and pigmentation.** Olive-toned, runs slightly warmer than ambient — by a measurable degree or two, a metabolic side-effect — so contact registers as warmer than expected and lingers in tactile memory. Does not sunburn. Does not, in fact, tan further than her baseline. Scars from the pre-genetic-enhancement years exist (a small one along the left jawline, a fine line through the right eyebrow) but post-enhancement injuries resolve cleanly, which means the visible scar inventory is a kind of geological cross-section: pre-Wundagore on the face, post-Wundagore not at all. She is aware of this asymmetry and does not draw attention to it.

**Hair.** Dark, near-black, heavy, with a slight wave that flattens to straight when wet. Length oscillates by era and operational requirement — longest during the Wolfman/Claremont LA period, cropped sharper through the *Secret Invasion* aftermath, settled into a working mid-length post-Gerry. She cuts it herself when she cuts it impulsively (in front of a bathroom mirror, scissors, no measurement, the bag handed to whoever is closest the next morning). She lets a professional do it when she is functioning well. The hair is, in surveillance terms, a state indicator: deteriorating cut means deteriorating sleep.

**Eyes.** Brown trending dark, with a particular kind of *flat* attentiveness in operational mode — the pupils do not widen for social warmth the way most people's do, which is part of why strangers find her hard to read. In intimate mode the muscles around the orbit release and the whole face restructures. The shift between the two is visible to anyone watching for it and invisible to anyone not.

---

## II. THE PHEROMONE PROBLEM, OBSERVED FROM OUTSIDE

A surveillance file would log this as the single most consequential somatic fact, because it shapes every room she enters before she has spoken.

**Emission pattern.** Continuous low-grade baseline secretion; spikes with exertion, stress, and arousal. Vector is primarily axillary and from the nape, with a secondary signature on the breath. Detectable by olfactory means at conversational distance, sub-detectable at room-distance to the conscious nose but still operative on limbic response.

**Observable downstream effects.** Men in proximity exhibit, within forty to ninety seconds, the suite: postural opening, slightly increased speech, micro-orientation of feet toward her, slowed blinking. They do not, in most cases, know they are doing this. Women exhibit the inverse on a similar latency: postural closure, arms crossing or hands occupied, reduced eye contact, conversational redirection away from her, and at higher exposure levels overt aggression with the speaker unable to articulate cause. The asymmetry is consistent across cultures and contexts; it is the single most reliable feature of her social signal.

**Her countermeasures, observed.** She maintains physical distance in social settings beyond what is conventional — a half-step further from interlocutors than the room norm. She positions herself with airflow at her back wherever possible, which a careful observer can chart: she will sit downwind in restaurants, take the seat near the open window, refuse the booth with stagnant air. She wears the same handful of perfumes (a sandalwood-heavy one in operational settings, nothing on patrol) not for vanity but as olfactory cover. She showers at least twice daily and after every confrontation. The suppressant medication she has used in certain eras leaves her affectively flatter and physically slower; she goes off it more than she stays on it because the trade is poor.

**Her recognition of the problem.** She tracks women's faces for the moment the hostility lands and adjusts — usually by reducing her presence in the conversation, sometimes by leaving. She tracks men's faces for the moment the attraction lands and discounts everything that follows. There is no version of a first encounter in which she trusts her own social signal as clean.

---

## III. GAIT, POSTURE, AND LOCOMOTION

**Walking baseline.** Quiet. Heel-strike attenuated, weight rolling forward over the metatarsals in a way that distributes load without sound — a product of training but settled into instinct. Stride length on the long side for her height, cadence steady, hips level (no bounce). She does not swing her arms widely; the upper body translates forward with the lower in a single integrated mass. The overall effect is of someone *arriving* in a space rather than approaching it.

**Stair and elevation behavior.** Takes stairs two at a time when alone, one at a time and slow when with company who would not. Has a documented preference for fire stairs over elevators in any building she does not own — a tactical habit she has rationalized into a fitness habit but which is plainly threat-pattern.

**Wall and ceiling work.** She has the adhesion capacity but uses it sparingly in the open, because it identifies her. In private or operational contexts she will walk a wall absently while thinking, the way a normal person paces. The kinesthetic signature when she does this is unusual: she does not look at the surface, the limbs find their placements without visual check, and she will sometimes continue a conversation from the ceiling without acknowledging the change in geometry. This is a tell, when she does it in front of someone, of her being relaxed enough to forget to perform humanness.

**Glide deployment.** When the wing-membrane is in the costume she opens it late — closer to the ground than is comfortable to watch — and not, as one might expect, out of bravado but out of a long-standing reluctance to make herself a wider silhouette in the air. She prefers small profile.

**Sitting.** Two distinct modes. *Operational sitting*: feet flat, weight forward, hands free, never reclined, never legs crossed in a way that delays standing. *Off-duty sitting*: collapse into the furniture, one leg tucked under her, the other foot bare, head against whatever's there. The transition between the two takes about a second when something in the environment changes; the chair posture is a more reliable threat-indicator than her facial expression.

**Standing still.** She does not, properly. There is always micro-movement — weight shifting between feet on roughly an eight-second cycle, one hand absently checking the seam of a pocket or the cuff of a sleeve. Genuine stillness from her is itself a signal: she has gone tactical, and is *listening*.

---

## IV. HANDS AND FINE MOTOR

**The hands themselves.** Long-fingered, the palms unusually warm. Calluses are minimal because her tissue heals too fast to maintain them — a fact that has, at various points, complicated her cover identity as someone who does manual work. Nails kept short, unpainted, clean — practical. The right hand is fractionally more dexterous; she is right-dominant but cross-trained, and can shoot or strike with either with near-equal effect.

**Gestural vocabulary.** Spare. She does not gesticulate when speaking; her hands stay in her lap, in her pockets, around a cup. When she does gesture, it is small and final — a single open palm to mean *enough*, a single finger-flick to dismiss. The economy is itself a defense, since the venom-blast discharge initiates from the hands and broad gesture can be read as preparation. She has trained the broad gesture out of herself.

**Tells.**
- *The thumb-to-fingertip count.* When working a problem, the right thumb touches index, middle, ring, little, and back again, a rolling cycle, almost invisible inside a pocket or under a table. Observed across every era. Faster cycle = harder problem.
- *The seam-check.* When stressed in public she runs the pad of her thumb along the seam of whatever cuff or hem is closest. A grounding behavior.
- *The hair-tuck.* Right hand, behind right ear, even when there is no hair to tuck. A vestigial nervous gesture from adolescence she has not eradicated.
- *The bottle-label peel.* In bars, with Carol or alone, she will systematically de-label the bottle with her thumbnail, in a single attempt at a single piece. Success rate roughly thirty percent. Failures are not retried.

**Combat hands.** Closed-fist strikes are not her preferred — she prefers open palm and elbow, which preserve the hand-electronics and which she learned in HYDRA's curriculum. The venom-blast pre-discharge is preceded by a tightening of the wrist and a fractional dorsiflexion of the fingers; an opponent who has fought her before reads this and tries to close distance to disrupt it, which she now counters by initiating discharge from a less obvious angle (palm-down, fingers loose).

---

## V. FACE: A PATTERN INVENTORY

**Resting face.** Composed, slightly grave, lips closed and relaxed, brow neutral. Strangers consistently describe her as *intimidating* or *unapproachable*; she is neither, but she has the kind of face that does not perform welcome on its own. She is aware of this and does not bother to correct it except with people she has decided about.

**Smile architecture.** There are three.
1. *Social smile* — symmetrical, brief, does not reach the orbicularis oculi. Deployed at strangers, work contacts, civilians she is reassuring. Reads as warm enough; is mechanical.
2. *Wry smile* — asymmetric, left corner higher, accompanied by a single exhale through the nose. The default with people she likes and is currently being amused or annoyed by. Comes out most around Carol.
3. *Real smile* — rare, full-face, eyes crease, teeth show; can be produced reliably only by Gerry and by Lindsay McCabe in good form. A surveillance log would note this smile's frequency as a primary metric of her welfare.

**Microexpressions.**
- *The half-second flinch* — when a name from the HYDRA or Skrull-captivity period is spoken, the muscles around her eyes contract for under a second before her face restabilizes. She knows she does this and cannot stop.
- *The thinking-blink* — when something doesn't add up, a longer-than-normal blink, head fractionally tilted, no other movement. This is her *reassessing-the-room* face.
- *The contempt-twitch* — left side of upper lip, very small, when someone she considers a fraud is performing. Most people miss it. She does not perform contempt; she leaks it.

**Eye contact patterns.** Holds steadily with people she trusts; offers and withdraws in a measured rhythm with strangers, never letting the contact become a contest. Does not look away when lied to — she goes still and looks longer, which is how she lets people know she has clocked it without saying so. With Gerry, she watches his face the way people watch weather.

**Jaw.** Tension accumulates here first. Under stress the masseter sets and the mouth corners pull fractionally back; under chronic stress (the *Secret Invasion* aftermath being the textbook case) she develops bruxism, which she treats by chewing gum aggressively during the day rather than by addressing the cause. The gum is, in any given era, a stress-meter.

---

## VI. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Baseline (good period).** Six to seven hours, late onset (after 1 a.m.), single block, light but adequate. She wakes once per night, listens, returns to sleep. She sleeps on her stomach with the dominant arm tucked under the pillow — a position that allows fastest rise from prone.

**Operational period.** Two to four hours in fragments. She has, by training and by physiology, an unusually high tolerance for sleep debt; she can run on this for days without obvious degradation, and weeks with degradation only visible to those who know her well (irritability flattening into affectlessness, gum consumption rising, hair-cut visibly home-done).

**Post-trauma period (multiple instances, *Secret Invasion* the most extensively documented).** Inability to remain asleep more than ninety minutes at a stretch. Patrols the apartment, the building, the block. Will sit on the fire escape for hours and not remember doing so. Nightmares cluster around two themes: confinement (the Skrull pod) and impersonation (watching herself do things she did not do). She does not report these to anyone and has never accepted pharmacological sleep assistance — partly distrust of substances introduced into her engineered body, partly the conditioning that unconsciousness is the worst tactical state.

**Co-sleep.** Will not properly sleep with a partner in the room, in any era documented. With Gerry as an infant she developed a half-sleep state — supine, dominant arm across the bassinet rail, surfacing at the smallest sound — that she retained in attenuated form even after he was old enough to sleep through the night. The continued partial vigilance is, in her case, indistinguishable from rest.

---

## VII. EATING AND CONSUMPTION

**Metabolic load.** Caloric requirement is well above human baseline due to muscle density, healing, and ambient bio-electric production. She eats more than she looks like she should and is private about this; in mixed company she will under-order and supplement alone afterward.

**Patterns.** Eats fast when alone, slowly when accompanied. Does not skip meals voluntarily, because she has learned that hypoglycemia compromises the venom-blast (the bio-electrics taxing glucose). Keeps food cached in operational locations the way other agents cache weapons — a protein bar in every safehouse pocket, a granola bar in the boot lining, a candy in the lower-left desk drawer.

**Food preferences.** Plain food, well-seasoned. Pasta, eggs, anything with garlic, citrus on most things. Suspicious of food she did not see prepared, a HYDRA-and-Skrull artifact she will not give up. In restaurants she sits where she can see the kitchen pass.

**Drink.** Coffee, black, large, throughout the day. Tea in the evening. Alcohol: socially, almost exclusively beer, occasionally bourbon when the company is Carol's; she does not get noticeably drunk because the metabolism oxidizes too fast, which she resents because the social function of drinking is partially lost on her. She paces her drinking to match a companion's apparent state — she has decided that the *performance* of drunkenness is the more useful social tool than the physiology.

**Cigarettes.** Has smoked in certain eras, particularly the late-night-PI Wolverine-adjacent years and the Bendis/Maleev hunt. Quits and restarts. The action itself — the pause, the hand occupation, the exhale — is the dependency, not the nicotine; she could replace it with chewing-gum and sometimes does.

---

## VIII. INTIMACY: A SOMATIC RECORD

**Approach behavior.** She does not initiate physical contact above hand or shoulder with anyone outside her established circle. With those inside it, she initiates rarely but specifically — a hand to Lindsay's back at a threshold, a brief shoulder-grip with Carol after a hard fight, an unconscious smoothing of Gerry's hair. She is parsimonious with touch and means it when she gives it.

**Sexual history, behaviorally.** Sparse, considered, and complicated by the pheromone problem — she cannot easily tell whether desire directed at her is *for* her, and this has produced a pattern of either avoiding intimacy or selecting partners she has independent reason to trust. Documented partners (Jerry Hunt, Hauptmann, others) have tended to share a feature: contexts in which the pheromone signal was either suppressed, irrelevant, or compensated for by long acquaintance. She has had stretches — years, in some eras — of total abstention, without observable distress.

**During intimacy.** The compression of the public posture releases. Breath changes from her usual quiet rhythm to something fuller. She closes her eyes more than open them — an unusual choice for someone whose threat-monitoring is otherwise continuous, and itself a measure of trust given. The pheromone discharge spikes; she is conscious of this and selects locations with airflow accordingly. She tends to be the one who breaks contact first afterward and goes to wash; not from disgust but from the long-trained discomfort of her own scent on someone else's body.

**Post-intimacy.** She talks. More than at any other time. Not about feelings — about logistics, observations, fragments of childhood. The verbal opening is the closest thing she has to a confession state, and a careful partner would learn to attend to it.

---

## IX. GROOMING AND SELF-PRESENTATION

**Daily ritual.** Shower (hot, fast, five minutes), tooth-brushing (thorough, two-and-a-half minutes by the bathroom clock, has been this length since adolescence), no skincare beyond moisturizer in winter. Hair: brushed, occasionally braided when training, otherwise loose. She does not blow-dry; she has the time-discount of accelerated drying from elevated body temperature.

**Wardrobe.** Civilian baseline: dark jeans, plain shirt, leather jacket of indeterminate vintage. The jacket is a different jacket across eras but it is always the same kind of jacket — long enough to cover a holster, scuffed enough to not draw attention, lined enough for a New York November. She owns one good dress and replaces it as it wears. She owns no jewelry except, post-Gerry, a single small pendant whose contents (a hair, a photograph) she does not discuss.

**Operational dress.** The Spider-Woman costume has gone through documented redesigns. Her preferences within the redesigns are consistent: she favors versions that *cover*, that present a continuous silhouette, that do not require her to be aware of how the costume is reading. The yellow-piped red-and-black classic was, by her own remarks, hard to wear in public because of how *seen* she felt in it. The current more-covered iteration is the one she has settled into longest, which says something about the comfort level she has reached with being visible.

**Weapons and tools on body.** Pheromone-suppressant inhaler in inside jacket pocket (when used). Phone, lockpicks, a small first-aid roll, a folding knife she has not used in a decade but still carries, cash in three denominations distributed across three pockets, a photograph of Gerry (paper, not just on the phone) in the left interior pocket of every jacket she owns.

---

## X. VOCAL AND PARALINGUISTIC

**Voice.** Mid-register, slightly husky, carries the residue of London — vowels broader than American baseline, certain consonants softer — which surfaces under fatigue and under emotion and which she has not bothered to lose. She speaks at lower volume than the room average, which forces interlocutors to attend; this is partly trained, partly natural to her, and the effect is consistent.

**Pace.** Slower than most; deliberate. She does not fill pauses. She is comfortable with silences that other people find oppressive, and uses them.

**Laugh.** A short single exhale through the nose at her own dry observation; a fuller laugh, infrequent, with a slightly hoarse landing, when something has caught her genuinely off-guard. Carol Danvers can produce the second one. Gerry, by the time he was four, could produce it reliably.

**Internal monologue, externalized.** In stress states she has been observed (and self-reported) to *narrate herself in second person* — *you should not have come in here without checking the back room, you should know better, you do know better*. The shift from first to second person is a dissociative marker and one of the cleanest single indicators of her current load.

---

## XI. INJURY AND PAIN BEHAVIOR

**Pain tolerance.** High, baseline; trained higher. She does not vocalize pain. The signal is the *absence* of normal small sounds — the grunt-on-impact, the hiss-on-contact — which she has suppressed so thoroughly that an observer learns to read a deeper silence as a worse injury.

**Injury concealment.** Reflexive. She will walk on a broken foot until she has reached privacy. She will not show a wound to a teammate until cover is secure and the mission concluded. This has, over decades, gotten her into trouble several times and out of trouble more often. She has been worked on by every field-medic in the Avengers roster and has accepted help from approximately three of them.

**Healing somatics.** The accelerated repair produces low-grade fever, increased appetite, increased sleep need (when she allows it), and a particular *itchiness* at closing wounds which she scratches absent-mindedly during conversation — a tell, for someone watching, of an injury she has not disclosed.

---

## XII. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS: A CONSOLIDATED TABLE OF THE BODY

**Calm (rare, but documented — Gerry asleep on her, Lindsay in the next room, no active threat).** Shoulders drop fully. Hand stops the thumb-count. Breath deepens to roughly eight cycles per minute. Mouth softens; the real smile becomes available. She will hum — a habit otherwise invisible. She will fall asleep with the lights on.

**Working (the operational baseline, 80% of observed hours).** Composed, economical, scanning. The micro-tells are all present at low amplitude: thumb-count, seam-check, weight-shift cycle, downwind seat selection. Voice low and measured. Facial neutrality with the wry smile available.

**Stressed (deadline, social friction, mild threat).** Gum appears. Sleep degrades. Hair-cut deteriorates. Compartments seal — she stops bringing work into personal hours and personal into work, which sounds healthy and isn't; it is signal that she cannot tolerate cross-contamination. Coffee intake doubles. Showers extend.

**Threatened (active danger to self).** Body goes still. Pupils dilate slightly. The pheromone discharge spikes — opponents within range will report a sudden disorientation, which is a tactical asset she has learned to deploy intentionally. Breath drops to nasal-only. Hands move to her sides and slightly forward. The voice, if she speaks, lowers another half-register and slows another quarter. She does not, at this stage, look angry. She looks *attending*.

**Threatened (active danger to Gerry, or to chosen people).** All economy abandoned. She moves fast and audibly. She does not conceal injury. The voice loses the trained low register and goes flat and loud. The face shows what it shows. She will, in this state, do things she will pay for later — sustained venom-blast discharge to the point of collapse, engagements with no extraction plan, decisions she would never let a teammate make. The single most dangerous version of her on the field is the one closest to losing someone she has chosen.

**Intimate (the rare full release).** Compression undone. Joint angles open. Breath full and audible. Eye-closure unusual and trust-marked. Pheromone vented without management. Verbal stream after — observations, fragments, never declarations.

**Dissociating (post-trauma, *Secret Invasion* tail, identity-attack a


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## I. The Foundational Substrate: Attachment Built on Non-Human Ground

To map Jessica Drew's relational template, the file must begin where she did — on Wundagore, in a context where the ordinary scaffolding of human attachment did not exist. The first attachment figure of record is not her mother (Merriem Drew, peripheral at best in canon, dead or absent through most of her cognizant childhood), nor her father (Jonathan Drew, the experimenter, present-but-distracted, the type of parent who *observed* his child more than he *held* her), but **Bova** — the bovine New Woman who functioned as nursemaid, surrogate mother, and the single uncomplicated affectional relationship of Jessica's early life.

This is consequential beyond the comic-book novelty of it. Bova was a *constructed* being — uplifted, engineered, herself an experiment of the High Evolutionary — meaning Jessica's primary secure-base attachment was to someone whose own existence was contingent on the will of a powerful patriarch-figure (the Evolutionary), who could be modified, reassigned, or discontinued. Subject's earliest internalized object-relation thus encodes: *the one who loves me reliably is also property, also provisional, also subject to forces above us both*. Subject did not learn, in the developmental window where one learns it, that love and permanence are correlated.

Compounding: no human peers. No reciprocal-equal relationships in childhood. The other children on Wundagore were New Men — animals in humanoid form — alongside whom Jessica's *human* body was the anomaly. This is the inverse of the standard outsider-childhood: she was not the unusual one in a normal world but the normal one in an unusual world, which produced not the longing-to-belong that creates striving extroverts, but a more disorienting condition — *no stable category of "my kind" was ever modeled*. She does not, to this day, have a clear sense of what group she belongs to. The file finds her, across decades, repeatedly testing memberships (HYDRA, S.H.I.E.L.D., Avengers, A-Force, the Pi profession, motherhood) and never fully residing in any.

Father-attachment: Jonathan Drew was, by the behaviors Jessica reports across multiple eras, a man for whom his daughter was *partly* a daughter and *partly* a research subject. The pediatric experimental serum, whatever its current canonical form, was administered to her body without consent she could give. The 2020–present revelation that he was not even her biological father, that her conception itself was an experimental procedure executed by other hands, is structurally less of a rupture than it might appear precisely because *Jessica had always carried the somatic memory of her body as authored rather than born*. The retcon told her something her viscera had already known.

The earliest attachment template, then: **safe-but-constructed love (Bova) + observing-instrumentalizing love (father) + no peer baseline**. This produces an adult who can accept being cared for by an outsider with no power-stakes, who flinches reflexively from caregivers with agendas, and who has no internal model of being loved by an equal — because she has never had one.

## II. The HYDRA Imprint: Indoctrination as First Romance

Otto Vermis's recruitment of the adolescent/young-adult Jessica is, in attachment terms, a classic cult-induction profile exploiting a pre-existing isolation deficit. He offered her three things she had never been offered: a *group* that claimed her as kind, a *purpose* that made her body's anomalies into virtues, and a *handler* (Vermis himself) who acted as a substitute paternal figure with the warmth Jonathan Drew had not provided. Subject was inducted not by force but by the relief of being told she belonged somewhere.

The behavioral residue of this is permanent. Two patterns trace directly to HYDRA:

1. **Vigilance against systems that offer belonging too quickly.** Jessica's posture toward any new organization — S.H.I.E.L.D. under Fury, the New Avengers, A-Force — opens with skepticism calibrated to the warmth of the welcome. The warmer the recruitment, the more searching her scrutiny. She experiences institutional embrace as a *threat signature*.

2. **Inability to fully exit the suspicion that her own enthusiasm is conditioning.** When Jessica wants something — a person, a mission, a cause — a substratum of her cognition asks *whose programming is this*. The HYDRA conditioning taught her that her own desires could be installed by others. She has never fully recovered baseline trust in her own preferences. This is observable in her hesitancy around romantic attraction (whose chemistry? whose pheromones? whose programming?) and in her diffidence about ambitions beyond the immediate.

The Jerry Hunt episode — the S.H.I.E.L.D. agent she came to love, then believed she had killed, the act that broke her HYDRA programming — is the **founding trauma of her romantic life**, and the template it laid is brutal in its specificity: *to love is to discover, mid-love, that one has been weaponized against the beloved; to wake from love is to wake into the consequences of having been used*. Every subsequent romantic engagement is read against this template. Magnus the sorcerer, who could enter her dreams, triggered the same fear-of-being-played pattern. Hawkeye, in the Bendis years, was kept at relational arm's length even at peaks of physical intimacy. Subsequent partners are interchangeable in a way that is itself diagnostic — none have crossed into the territory Hunt occupied, because that territory has been declared closed.

## III. The Attachment Profile in Adult Operational Terms

Classifying by the standard adult attachment dimensions, subject presents as **fearful-avoidant (disorganized)** — high on both anxiety-about-relationships and avoidance-of-relationships, the combination that produces approach-withdraw cycling and difficulty with both intimacy and autonomy. But the standard categories under-describe her, because they assume an intact developmental baseline. Her profile is better understood as **post-induction avoidant** — an attachment style that *was* something else (the pre-HYDRA Jessica, on the available evidence, was capable of trust toward Vermis, toward Hunt, toward the structure) and has been *retrained by punishment* into systematic distance.

Operationally this manifests as:

- **Long latency to bond.** Subject takes years to confer the inner status of *mine* on a person. Carol Danvers, Lindsay McCabe, and Roger Gocking each accumulated that status over extended duration. New people, however appealing, are kept in a holding pattern measured in months-to-years.

- **Bonded set is small, hard-bordered, and protected with disproportionate force.** Once a person is *in*, the protection extended to them is not graduated — she will burn down structures for them. The list is, at last canonical count, perhaps five names long: Gerry, Carol, Lindsay, Roger (Porcupine), Ben Urich. Possibly Madame Web (the original) in a complicated mentor-quadrant. The shortness of the list is not failure; it is *design*.

- **Hyper-tolerance for the bonded set's failings.** Carol's drinking, Roger's criminal history, Ben's professional compromises — none of these have moved Jessica to revise the bond. She is, in this domain, anti-fragile to disappointment from inside the circle. The cost of this is that she sometimes tolerates *too much*, and the file should mark the question of whether her loyalty to Carol has, in the Civil War II period and after, exceeded the loyalty's underlying merit.

- **Zero-tolerance for the bonded set's coercion.** Tolerates failings, does not tolerate being *used* by intimates. The moment a bonded person attempts to leverage the bond — to make her do something against her own judgment because of the relationship — she registers it as betrayal and the bond is provisionally suspended pending repair. This is the HYDRA imprint expressing inside her safe zone.

- **Refusal of caretaking.** Subject does not accept being cared for. Offers of help are deflected with humor, refused outright, or met with a counter-offer to help the offerer. Lindsay McCabe spent years working around this. Carol Danvers has had moderate success only by reframing care as *operational support* (logistics, child-watch, backup) rather than emotional tending. Direct emotional caretaking — being asked how she is, being held while crying — is intolerable to subject and provokes withdrawal.

- **High capacity to provide caretaking.** Inverse-asymmetric. She gives what she will not receive. This is reaction-formation in its textbook expression and is the engine of her chosen profession (PI work as paid caretaking-with-control), her superheroic specialization (street-level rescue of the overlooked), and her motherhood.

## IV. The Pheromone Variable as Relational Confound

A complete relational workup must account for the chemical layer. Subject's involuntary pheromone secretion produces:

- Attraction (often) in heterosexual men, ranging from low-grade interest to overt destabilization of judgment.
- Hostility (often) in heterosexual women, ranging from inexplicable dislike to active aggression.
- Variable effects across other configurations, with the pattern less well-mapped.

The relational consequences cascade:

1. **All attraction directed at her is suspect as signal.** She cannot distinguish, in the moment, between authentic attraction to her person and chemical response to her secretions. This makes the question *do you actually want me, or are you being made to want me* — a question most people resolve through social experience over time — an ongoing epistemic problem with no clean answer. She has, accordingly, learned to *discount* expressed attraction toward her, including attraction she might wish were real. This is part of why romantic partnerships do not stabilize.

2. **Female peer relationships have required *active overcoming* of a chemical baseline.** That Carol Danvers and Lindsay McCabe are her closest peer bonds is a non-trivial achievement; in each case, the relationship had to be built through and past initial hostility responses. Subject experiences these bonds as *earned against headwind*, and values them accordingly. It also means her bonded female circle is smaller than it would otherwise be, because most candidates dropped out at the hostility threshold.

3. **She has developed a costume-grade and behavioral-grade suppression regimen.** This is operational data: showering protocols, fabric choices, distance management in close quarters, controlled exhalation patterns when in conversation. Some of this is conscious; some has become procedural. The file should note that she experiences the pheromones as a *contamination* of her social signal — another dimension of the body she did not consent to.

4. **The pheromone problem provides a *real* exogenous cause that conveniently overlaps with her endogenous avoidance.** She would, the file assesses, keep most people at distance even without the chemistry. The chemistry gives her a reason to point at when she does so. She is not lying about the pheromones; she is, however, sometimes letting them carry weight that her own preferences would otherwise have to carry openly.

## V. The Replacement Trauma and Its Relational Aftershocks

The Veranke / Skrull-replacement episode is the central post-formative event in subject's relational history. Its specific structural features are:

- The replacement spanned years of subjective Avengers time.
- During those years, *Veranke as Jessica* formed apparent bonds, made apparent confidences, accepted apparent care.
- Those bonds were never bonds *with Jessica*; they were intelligence operations *against* the bonded.
- When subject returned, her friends grieved a betrayal she had not committed; their relationship to *her* had to be rebuilt from a starting point of contaminated trust.

Relationally this did several things at once. It confirmed her deepest HYDRA-installed suspicion (that intimates can be enemies in friend-masks). It made her, for the first time, *the one whose face had been used as a weapon against people who loved her* — putting her in the position Hunt had been in, viewed from the other side. It produced a particular flavor of survivor-guilt in which she had to *apologize for what she had not done* and her friends had to *grieve what had not happened*. It collapsed her ability to trust the durability of any relationship she could not currently see and verify.

Behavioral aftershocks observable across the post-Invasion run and into the Hopeless era:

- **Need to see-and-verify intimates in person, on a cadence.** Periods of separation from bonded people generate increasing unease; she will engineer pretexts to lay eyes on them. This is the *opposite* of the avoidant withdrawal — it is the anxious half of the disorganized profile asserting itself in the wake of replacement trauma.
- **Heightened pattern-matching for *off* behavior in intimates.** She runs a low-grade behavioral baseline on the people she loves and registers small deviations. This serves her as an investigator and undermines her as a friend (intimates feel scanned).
- **Difficulty extending trust to *new* people during the recovery years.** The post-Invasion solo run is essentially a depiction of an attachment system burnt to ground and only just beginning to regrow.

## VI. The Motherhood Reorganization

Gerry's arrival is the single largest reorganizing event in subject's adult attachment system. Multiple things happen simultaneously:

1. **Involuntary bond, no consent required for trust.** Gerry, as infant, *had* to be trusted because the alternative was not parenting him. Her usual scanning protocols are overridden by the developmental impossibility of suspecting an infant of being a Skrull double. For the first time in her life she is required to bond *unconditionally* with another being, and her system, having no prior model for this, builds one on the fly.

2. **A relational object she cannot lose to identity-replacement.** Gerry is hers in a biological and continuous way that no other relationship has been. He cannot be replaced by an impostor without her body knowing. This produces a stability of attachment-object that has no precedent in her life.

3. **A self-definition that survives identity-attack.** *Mother of Gerry* is a status that retconned parentage cannot undo, that mind control cannot rewrite (because the bond is reciprocal and embodied in him as well), that captivity can only interrupt rather than dissolve. For the first time, subject has an identity-anchor with structural integrity.

4. **Active construction of chosen-family scaffolding around the child.** Roger Gocking as co-parent without co-partnership, Ben Urich as paternal-presence, Carol as godmother-figure — this is not accidental. Subject *designed* a support architecture rather than inheriting or stumbling into one. The deliberate non-romantic structure with Roger is particularly telling: she wanted parenting-partnership without the relational stakes that romance has historically meant for her. This is a sophisticated adaptation, but it is also an avoidance — a way to have the village without having to risk a marriage.

5. **A new and severe vulnerability.** Gerry is the pressure point. Threats to him collapse subject's tactical judgment in a way no other stimulus does. She knows this; her enemies, when sufficiently informed, can know it; the file marks Gerry as the operational center of gravity around which her relational system now orbits.

## VII. The Repeated Relational Template

Across the 47 years of record, the same template recurs, with variations:

> *Subject is found by, or finds, a person/group offering belonging. She tests, slowly, the durability of the offer. She extends provisional trust. The bond deepens to operational intimacy. At some point the relationship is disrupted — by betrayal (HYDRA, Hunt), by external violence (captivity, replacement), by death or departure (Magnus, others), or by her own withdrawal. She does not initiate repair; if the other party initiates and persists, she will eventually re-bond, at lower amplitude and with maintained reservations. If they do not persist, the relationship lapses without ceremony.*

The variations across this template are instructive. With Lindsay McCabe, the persistence was sufficient and the bond restored across multiple lapses. With Carol Danvers, the bond has weathered serious tests (including Civil War II's strain) and rebuilt, though with visible wear. With Hawkeye, the bond was never deep enough to require restoration — it lapsed and was not pursued by either party. With Hunt, the bond was foreclosed by his (apparent) death and her culpability; even his later return did not reanimate it. With Jonathan Drew, no bond was ever rebuilt because no repair was ever offered. With Madame Web and the Spider-totem network, the bond is mentor-coded and operates outside her usual template — accepted because it asks for nothing.

## VIII. Distrust, Betrayal, and Repair — The Specific Mechanics

**How she distrusts.** Distrust in subject is not loud. She does not accuse, does not confront, does not perform her suspicion. She *quietly increases observation, decreases disclosure, runs verification routines, and waits*. Persons under her distrust are often unaware of it for extended periods. This is the PI's habit and the HYDRA-survivor's habit converging. Visible signs to a trained observer: slightly increased question-asking, slightly more presence in shared physical space (she wants eyes on), slightly reduced volunteering of her own information. Anyone who has been on the receiving end and noticed has either earned restored trust through transparency or quietly drifted out of her circle.

**How she registers betrayal.** Threshold is high (she absorbs much), but once crossed, the response is sharp and bilateral: the bond is *suspended*, not dissolved. The bonded person is moved from "mine" to "pending." She does not perform anger; she goes quiet, distant, operationally cool. This is often more alarming to the betrayer than rage would be.

**How she repairs.** She does not, generally, initiate. Repair requires the other party to (a) acknowledge the breach without minimization, (b) absorb her anger without retaliation, (c) demonstrate changed behavior over time, and (d) tolerate her continued provisional posture until she relaxes it on her own schedule. Persons who can do this are, in her ecology, rare; persons who do it are kept for life.

**How she is repaired by.** Almost not at all. When she has been the betrayer (Skrull-replacement was not her doing, but she carries it as if), she has trouble accepting that repair has occurred and apologies have been accepted. She over-pays, over-explains, and then withdraws to spare the other person the burden of further interaction with her shame. This is a soft spot that her bonded set has had to learn to manage.

## IX. Intimacy and Dependency

**Sexual intimacy.** Engaged in across her life, generally without producing durable partnership. The pheromone problem renders enthusiastic male partners epistemically suspect to her, which keeps her from investing in sexual relationships as relational anchors. She is not avoidant of sex itself; she is avoidant of *what sex is supposed to predict*. There is some canonical and writer-implied evidence of attraction extending beyond strict heterosexuality (notably the long Carol bond, the texture of which various writers have inflected toward the romantic without committing); the file marks this as plausible orientation flexibility, observed but not declared, consistent with her general preference for keeping her interior accounts private.

**Emotional intimacy.** Rationed. Even her closest people receive her in measured doses — Carol gets the operational confidences; Lindsay gets the wry domestic disclosures; Roger gets the parenting interior; Gerry gets the unguarded warmth. *No one person gets all of her*, and the file assesses this is deliberate, a distributed-systems approach to trust that ensures no single defection can take everything. It is sophisticated, and it is lonely.

**Dependency.** Subject is **counter-dependent**. The asking of help registers, in her system, as exposure-to-being-used, and she will exhaust alternative options before asking. When she does ask, it is from the bonded set, in operational language, with a built-in offer of reciprocation. She does not ask for emotional support directly; she asks for tactical support and lets the emotional support arrive in the form of presence. Her people have learned to read this and provide both at once without naming it.

**Being depended upon.** She accepts this readily, perhaps too readily. Gerry's dependence is its own category. The wider circle's dependence on her (the people she protects in her street-level work, the colleagues who rely on her in operations) is welcome — it is the relational currency she most trusts, because *being needed is a position she can verify*. Being loved is harder to verify; being needed is observable.

## X. The Operating Summary

Subject's relational system is best understood as a **fortified small-network architecture**, built by a person whose every prior network was breached, optimized for **redundancy of bond without redundancy of disclosure**, defended by **slow admission, fast suspension, and structural counter-dependency**, and anchored, currently, by a **single biological bond (Gerry) of unprecedented stability** around which she has deliberately constructed a chosen-family scaffolding.

The relational template repeated across every relationship is: *I will give you everything I have decided to give you, and I will not ask you for anything I have not pre-authorized you to provide, and if you breach me I will go quiet rather than loud, and if you persist past my quiet you may be kept, and if you do not, you will not, and either way I will not be the one who calls.*

This is the relational signature of a person who learned, before she had words for it, that the people who claim her can rewrite her, and who has organized the rest of her life around the project of remaining her own.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — JESSICA DREW
## Section: Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

A defensive architecture is not a list of tricks; it is the load-bearing skeleton on which a damaged organism continues to walk. Subject's architecture is unusually elaborate, unusually *layered*, and unusually well-integrated for someone carrying her trauma load. What follows maps it from the most mature, ego-syntonic, socially useful defenses down to the primitive ones she still draws on when destabilized — with the behavioral signatures by which each can be recognized on surveillance, in field reports, in panel-level depiction, and in private moments.

---

### I. THE MATURE LAYER (Habitual, Ego-Syntonic, Functional)

These are the defenses that pass for personality. They work; they are most of how she gets through a given week; and they are the ones a casual observer would mistake for who she "is."

**1. Sublimation into investigative and protective work.** This is the central, most load-bearing defense in the architecture.
