The PI license she took after depowerment (Wolfman/Gruenwald-era Los Angeles years, the long Lindsay McCabe partnership) and the street-level reorientation of the Hopeless run are not job choices — they are channels for hypervigilance, mistrust, and rage that would otherwise corrode her. Investigation lets her *act on* her belief that institutions lie without becoming a paranoid; protection of the overlooked lets her *enact* the rescue she did not receive without having to ask for it from anyone else. The behavioral signature is that the work intensifies when other regulators fail — patrol routes lengthen during the weeks she is not sleeping, case intake spikes after relational disappointments, and the moral selectivity of her cases tightens (more cases involving missing women, trafficked children, surveilled persons — the populations whose situations isomorph with hers).

**2. Humor — specifically dry, observational, self-deflating, well-timed.** Her humor is among the most consistent traits across forty-seven years of writers, surviving Wolfman, Claremont, Bendis, Hopeless, and Pacheco intact, which is itself diagnostic — it is *her* defense, not a writer's voice. Functionally it does three things: (a) pre-empts other people's discomfort by acknowledging it first, defusing the pheromone problem socially; (b) allows her to say true and painful things while marking them as not-requiring-a-response, protecting her from the vulnerability of being taken seriously; (c) maintains internal distance from her own circumstance, preventing affect from overwhelming function. The tells: humor *increases* with stress, not decreases; the jokes get drier and more clipped as fear rises; she will land a line at the moment a less defended person would be crying.

**3. Altruism, specifically toward chosen marginal populations.** This is sublimation's twin, but it is worth separating because it points outward rather than inward. Her construction of a chosen family around Gerry — Roger Gocking, Ben Urich, Carol Danvers in an aunt-role — and her selection of cases that center women, children, and the institutionally invisible, is altruism in the technical Vaillant sense: a mature defense that converts her own unmet needs into a project for others, and derives stable narcissistic supply from the project's success. The risk is the one all altruistic defenders run — depletion without resupply, because accepting care for herself remains the structurally untrained move.

**4. Anticipation.** She runs scenarios. Surveillance-grade observation of her work pattern shows the habit constantly: route variation, exit-mapping on entering any room, predictive modeling of how a given operation could go wrong, contingency loadouts. This is mature because it is *bounded* — she anticipates, prepares, and then proceeds — rather than degenerating into rumination or paralysis. Origin: HYDRA training laid the technical substrate; Skrull captivity supplied the conviction that *the bad outcome is the likely one*. Behavioral signature: she is almost never surprised by betrayal, almost always surprised by sincerity.

**5. Suppression (as opposed to repression).** She can put things down on purpose. She can decide not to think about the Skrull pod until Tuesday, and on Tuesday she will think about it, and Wednesday she will go to work. This is the defense that distinguishes the high-functioning C-PTSD survivor from the disabled one, and she has it. Evidence: the relatively brief functional impairment between *Secret Invasion* #8 and operational return; the equanimity with which she received the Pacheco/Perez parentage retcon (she registered it, processed it, and continued). The cost is that suppressed material does not disappear — it routes into the insomnia, the patrol patterns, the bio-electric discharge thresholds, the rationing of intimacy.

---

### II. THE NEUROTIC MIDDLE LAYER (Workable, Sometimes Costly)

These cost more than they yield in the long run, but in the short run they are how she keeps moving.

**6. Intellectualization.** Pervasive. She translates affect into analysis, feeling into casework, fear into protocol. The clearest behavioral expression is the way she debriefs herself — even internally — using the vocabulary of operations rather than the vocabulary of emotion. She will say *the situation deteriorated* rather than *I was terrified*. In conversation with Carol she occasionally breaks frame and uses feeling-words; with almost no one else. This is the defense that lets her be in the same room as her history without dissolving, and it is also why she sometimes misses what is happening to her until it is well underway.

**7. Compartmentalization.** Distinct seals between (a) Spider-Woman the operative, (b) Jessica Drew the investigator, (c) Gerry's mother, (d) Carol's friend, (e) the historical archive of HYDRA-asset and Skrull-captive selves. Each compartment has its own affect register, its own clothing, its own physical posture, its own permitted topics. The seals are deliberate and they are *maintained* — she does not, for example, bring Spider-Woman analysis to mothering decisions, and she does not bring Gerry into operational thinking until forced. The failure mode is well-documented: when threats penetrate a compartment they *do not* trigger graceful integration, they trigger catastrophic priority collapse — every other compartment instantly subordinates to the breached one, usually Gerry's, and her tactical judgment degrades accordingly. Surveillance signature of healthy compartmentalization: code-switching in vocal register, posture, gait, even pheromone-control discipline, depending on which compartment is active.

**8. Reaction formation around caretaking.** The person who was failed by every protector becomes the protector who does not fail. Cleanly diagnostic: she will extend to others (a frightened witness, a runaway, Gerry, a depowered colleague) the exact pattern of presence, patience, and non-abandonment she never received. The defense is workable because the caretaking is *real* and the people *are* helped; the cost is that it forecloses her own request for care, since the role she has organized her identity around does not include being the one receiving it. Carol Danvers is one of the very few people in canon who has trained Jessica to receive care, and even that took years and required Carol to override Jessica's deflection rituals repeatedly.

**9. Displacement of anger into precision violence.** Anger is the affect she manages least well — not because she explodes (she does not), but because she cannot *release* it once activated. The displacement runs from the originating object (HYDRA, Skrulls, her father-figures, the institutions that handled her) to the proximate operational target. The behavioral signature is the specific quality of her violence under elevated anger states: cold, surgical, sustained past tactical necessity, with a slight delay in disengagement when the fight is over. The post-Invasion arc is the cleanest extant record of this defense running long; she hunted Skrull remnants past the operational justification for doing so because the hunt was metabolizing the rage.

**10. Identification with the aggressor — partial, controlled, instrumentalized.** A subtler defense that she runs deliberately rather than automatically: she retains the HYDRA tradecraft, the assassin's economy of movement, the operational vocabulary, and uses them in service of opposite ends. This is not pure identification (which would mean becoming what hurt her); it is the *selective retention of the predator's competencies under the prey's value system*. The risk is that under sufficient stress the value system can slip and the competencies persist. She has not actually crossed that line in canon; she has come near it (Skrull-hunt period) and recognized it as a near miss, which is itself evidence of intact reflective function.

**11. Isolation of affect.** Distinct from intellectualization: where intellectualization replaces feeling with thought, isolation of affect *retains the cognitive content of an event while stripping its emotional valence*. She can describe her captivity, her brainwashing, her father's experimentation, in flat clinical language. Listeners often mistake this for resolution. It is not resolution; it is a defense that allows the material to be discussed without re-traumatizing the discusser, and it has been refined over decades.

---

### III. THE PRIMITIVE LAYER (Engaged Under High Load)

These come online when the upper layers fail. They are the defenses that betray how badly she has been hurt.

**12. Depersonalization / derealization.** The recurrent second-person internal narration in the Bendis/Maleev *Spider-Woman* work — *you walk into the bar, you order a drink you won't finish, you watch the door* — is a depersonalization defense made textual. She steps outside herself and observes the subject of her life from a slight remove. This was a literal somatic event in *Spider-Woman* #50 (soul-body separation) and recurs functionally under post-Invasion stress, post-captivity stress, and during operations whose targets resemble her original conditioning. The defense is protective in the short term (the body endures what the observer-self does not have to feel) and corrosive in the long term (the observer-self begins to be the only self that feels real).

**13. Counterphobic action.** When frightened, *toward* the threat, alone. This is the defense that has nearly killed her more times than any tactical error. It is recognizable on surveillance as a specific decision-tree degradation: faced with a threat that should prompt consultation, she instead computes the path of solo confrontation, and the more frightened she is the more confident she becomes that solo is correct. The fear is converted into operational forward-momentum. Origin: in HYDRA, the safe move was to *act*, because hesitation was punished; the conditioning persists. The defense is primitive because it is non-reflective and it does not allow her to be helped.

**14. Withdrawal — geographic, social, communicative.** She disappears. The Los Angeles years, the long quiet periods between book runs, the patrol-night patterns: each is in part a chosen-aloneness deployed defensively. The withdrawal is *managed* (she rarely vanishes from people she has committed to, especially Gerry), but its presence is the surveillance tell that an upper-layer defense has failed and she is rationing exposure until she can rebuild. The cost is that withdrawal extends and the rebuild gets harder; the durability of the Carol Danvers relationship is partly because Carol has learned not to retaliate against the withdrawals.

**15. Somatization, narrow form.** Less prominent than in other complex-trauma profiles because her body was never baseline — she has no normal somatic register to which symptoms can announce themselves contrastively. What does appear: the chronic insomnia (Bendis/Maleev, Hopeless runs), tension headaches under operational load, occasional involuntary pheromone spikes during high affect (which she has learned to read as an early-warning system that her regulation is slipping), and a slight increase in bio-electric discharge threshold sensitivity under stress (overcharge events in combat correlate with high-affect periods).

**16. Splitting — limited, situational, never characterological.** She does not split people into all-good/all-bad as a stable pattern (this is one of the strongest pieces of evidence against a BPD reading). She *does* engage limited situational splitting against institutions and against persons who have demonstrably betrayed her — HYDRA becomes uniformly malign, Skrulls become uniformly malign, certain handlers (Fury at moments) become unredeemable. The split is reality-grounded but it is overextended past the data. It is primitive because it is categorical and resistant to revision; it is bounded because it does not generalize to her intimates.

**17. Acting out — rare, tightly controlled.** When defenses stack-fail, she does not break down; she does an operation she should not do. The Skrull-hunt overreach is the cleanest example. The behavior discharges what cannot be metabolized. It looks like agency from outside; it is closer to compulsion from inside. The fact that it presents as competent operational behavior is what makes it dangerous and what makes it hard to interrupt — no one watching, including her, recognizes it as a symptom.

---

### IV. POSITIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Constructed, Maintained, Working)

Distinct from defenses: these are *built structures* she has erected in the world that compensate for what was taken from her. They are the closest she has to repair.

**18. Chosen-family construction.** The single most adaptive thing she has done in her adult life. The deliberate assembly of an unconventional support network around Gerry — Roger as co-parent without romantic entanglement (rationed proximity), Ben Urich as elder-witness, Carol as anchor — is a structural workaround for her attachment damage. Each member was selected for the specific feature of *accepting her before needing anything from her and tolerating her withdrawals without retaliation*. This is the criterion she cannot articulate but reliably applies. The network is small, durable, and functions as the secure base she could not generate from her family of origin.

**19. Motherhood as identity ballast.** Gerry has provided the first stable answer to *who am I*. The answer — *I am Gerry's mother* — is load-bearing and is therefore both her greatest source of organization and her greatest single vulnerability. Compensatory because it gives her an identity that *cannot be retconned away by an enemy*: the relationship is enacted daily, the child is real, the role is not contingent on origin story.

**20. Professional competence as identity ballast.** What she does, she does well; what she does well, no Skrull, no brainwashing, and no parentage revision can take from her. Competence is the one form of self-knowledge she has not had to surrender. She invests in it accordingly.

**21. Dark humor as social lubricant.** Already noted as a defense; also a *compensation*, because it constructs a social surface that lets her remain in rooms she would otherwise have to leave.

**22. The personal moral code.** In the absence of trustable institutions or ideologies, she has built a portable, personally maintained ethical framework — empirical, case-by-case, weighted toward the protection of the overlooked. It is compensatory because it gives her *a stable ought* in the absence of stable belonging. She can act morally without belonging to anything that tells her how, which is rare and hard-won.

---

### V. NEGATIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Habits That Pass As Coping)

**23. Workaholism / patrol-as-sleep-substitute.** The night routes are not strictly operational. They are a way to fill the hours she cannot sleep without acknowledging that she cannot sleep. The cost is cumulative under-recovery and degraded judgment at the tail of long stretches.

**24. Reflexive single-handed problem-solving.** Consultation is structurally available — Carol is one call away, the broader Avengers network is responsive — and she does not use it. The reflex is to compute the solo path first and the consultation path as fallback. This is a compensation for the historical fact that asking has been punished; it is negative because the conditions that made it adaptive no longer apply and she has not updated.

**25. Acclimation to loneliness.** She tolerates being alone exceptionally well. This is presented in casual reading as strength; clinically it is concerning, because acclimation to a deprivation is not the same as not needing the thing. The cost is that the threshold at which she registers loneliness as a problem worth addressing has been pushed so high that by the time she notices, repair is expensive.

**26. Under-reporting of injury, both physical and psychological.** Field after-actions consistently understate damage taken. This is partly operational discipline and partly a deeper habit of treating her own state as low-priority information. The pattern extends to the psychological: she does not bring her injuries to the people who would help with them until they are well past the point of easy treatment.

**27. The pheromone problem as deployable alibi.** The pheromones are a real biological fact and a real social disability — and they are also, secondarily, an *externalized explanation she can deploy for distances she may want for other reasons*. When intimacy threatens, the pheromone story is always available: *people can't really be near me, it's chemical*. The defense lets her decline closeness without owning the decline. It is negative because it forecloses the test of whether closeness might actually be possible with a given person if attempted.

---

### VI. STRUCTURAL OBSERVATIONS

The architecture overall is **upper-layer-dominant**: most days, most weeks, most years, she runs on sublimation, humor, altruism, anticipation, and suppression, and these are sufficient. The middle layer activates under predictable load (operations, anniversaries, identity-attacks, threats to chosen people). The primitive layer activates rarely but recognizably — depersonalized narration, counterphobic solo action, geographic withdrawal — and serves as the surveillance early-warning that something has overrun her usual capacity.

The architecture's strengths: redundancy (multiple defenses cover the same load), maturity (most defenses are Vaillant-high), and integration with prosocial behavior (her defenses generally help others rather than only herself).

The architecture's weaknesses: (a) it is built around *not asking* — every defense in it lets her endure without requesting aid, and the one circumstance she is poorly defended against is one in which she would have to ask; (b) it is built around *Gerry as ballast* — the load on the motherhood compartment is structurally excessive, and any sustained threat to Gerry will exceed the architecture's design tolerances; (c) it is built around *competence as identity* — a sustained failure of competence (incapacitation, depowerment of a kind that prevents the protective work) would deprive her of the primary mechanism by which she knows who she is.

The architecture is, in the aggregate, the work of someone who has rebuilt herself from the inside more times than most people are asked to do once, and who has learned — slowly, expensively, and not entirely — that the rebuild is possible. That knowledge is itself her most adaptive possession, and it is the one no enemy has yet found a way to take.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE: JESSICA DREW

## Preface: The Methodological Problem

Any decade-by-decade psychological mapping of this subject must begin with a frank acknowledgment of the structural difficulty: her published life contains at least two extended periods in which the "Jessica Drew" of record was not, in fact, Jessica Drew (the Skrull replacement spanning roughly *New Avengers* #1 onward through *Secret Invasion* #8), and at least three periods in which her own memories of who she was were subsequently revealed to be implanted, falsified, or biographically incorrect (HYDRA conditioning under Vermis; retconned parentage in the Pacheco/Perez run; episodic possession and mind-influence events scattered through the Wolfman, Claremont, and Bendis runs). What follows therefore tracks not a single continuous developmental line but a series of *psychological reconstructions* — the subject rebuilding a workable self from each successive collapse, with each rebuild bearing scar tissue from the prior one.

The frameworks deployed here are: Bowlby/Ainsworth/Main attachment theory (with Hesse and Main's disorganized/fearful-avoidant elaboration); Pierre Janet's dissociation model as updated by van der Hart, Nijenhuis, and Steele (the structural dissociation of the personality, or SDP, model); Judith Herman's complex trauma stage model; Linehan's biosocial theory for affect dysregulation; and Vaillant's hierarchy of defenses (mature/neurotic/immature/psychotic) for tracking defensive maturation across time.

---

## Childhood and Adolescence (Wundagore through HYDRA induction; pre-1977 backstory, dramatized intermittently across all eras)

**Affect regulation.** The pre-HYDRA child had no normative socialization template for affect. Her closest attachment figure was Bova, a non-human caretaker, and her peer environment consisted of the High Evolutionary's New Men — beings whose own affect was unstable and whose social rules were idiosyncratic. The result is that she never internalized standard human emotional reciprocity in the developmental window when such internalization is cheap. She learned later, by observation and rehearsal, what other children acquire by osmosis. This produces, even in adulthood, a slight observational lag in her social processing — she can be seen, in the Hopeless run especially, doing the visible cognitive work of reading a room rather than just feeling it.

**Cognitive style.** The early environment was scientifically saturated. The High Evolutionary's compound was effectively a laboratory in which she was both ward and specimen. The cognitive style she absorbed was *empirical, instrumentalist, and skeptical of given categories* — fitting for a child who watched animals become humans and who herself was an experimental subject. This is the substrate of her later investigator's mind.

**Self-concept.** Functionally absent. With no peers of her own kind, no mother, and a father whose attention was filtered through his work, she did not have the relational mirroring necessary for a coherent early self. The body she lived in was non-baseline and pheromonally aberrant — she would have registered, pre-verbally, that adults responded to her in patterned but unexplained ways (male warmth, female aversion) that no caregiver helped her interpret. This is a classic substrate for later identity diffusion: a child who learns that she elicits responses she cannot predict or control develops a self-concept built around *being-acted-upon* rather than acting.

**Attachment formation.** Insecure from the start, with strong avoidant features. Janet's structural dissociation model would predict, given a developmental environment this anomalous, the early formation of segregated emotional/behavioral parts — an Apparently Normal Part oriented toward daily functioning and Emotional Parts holding the affect that the environment could not metabolize. This is the architecture HYDRA later exploited.

**HYDRA induction (late adolescence).** Vermis's grooming was textbook destructive-cult methodology: love-bombing into a "family" structure, false biographical narrative (the spider-evolution myth), behavioral conditioning, and a romantic pair-bond (with the man she was conditioned to believe was a HYDRA loyalist, then ordered to kill) engineered as both reward and severance test. Her psychological vulnerability to this was high precisely because she had no prior secure attachment to compare it against. The rupture — believing she had killed Jerry Hunt — was her first adult experience of *being weaponized against someone she loved by an authority she had trusted*. This is the foundational template for every subsequent betrayal-pattern she will scan for across the next five decades.

---

## The First Solo Decade (roughly 1977–1983, *Marvel Spotlight* #32 through *Avengers* #240–241)

**Affect regulation.** Volatile in private, controlled in public. The Wolfman/Gruenwald/Fleisher run depicts a subject who is frequently in tears alone in apartments — Los Angeles especially — but who in operational situations is flat-affect and tactical. This is the classical structural-dissociation split: the working self is anesthetized; the affect lives in compartments accessible only when alone and unobserved. She does not yet possess mature affect regulation. What she has is *containment by isolation*: she rations her own feelings by rationing her own social exposure.

**Cognitive style.** Suspicious, ruminative, prone to self-pathologizing attribution. She defaults, when rejected, to "I am the wrong one" rather than "this situation is hostile" — a depressogenic attributional style in Seligman's sense, internal-stable-global. The Claremont issues lean into this hard; her internal monologue repeatedly returns to the question of whether she is human enough to deserve company.

**Self-concept.** *Monstrous and provisional.* This is the period in which her self-concept is most explicitly negative. She refers to herself, in internal monologue, as something other than a person more than once. The *Spider-Woman* #50 soul/body separation is the symbolic apex: her subjective experience of being one thing inside a body that is another thing made literal. The pheromone problem is integrated into her self-concept not as a neutral physiological fact but as evidence of contamination — women hate her *because there is something wrong with her*, and men's attraction is read as further evidence that she cannot trust her own desirability.

**Attachment behavior.** Approach-avoidance cycling. She forms intense quick bonds (Magnus, Hunt-figures, Lindsay McCabe early) and then either withdraws geographically (relocations between London, Los Angeles, San Francisco) or finds reason to mistrust the bond. Lindsay is the first relationship that *survives* this cycling, because Lindsay simply does not retaliate against her withdrawals — a behavioral discovery that becomes a template.

**Defensive hierarchy.** Predominantly immature and neurotic per Vaillant. Heavy reliance on *isolation of affect*, *somatization* (the headaches and exhaustion that recur in this run), *acting out* (geographic flight), and *reaction formation* (defending strangers in ways she cannot defend herself). Sublimation begins to appear toward the end of the run as she folds existential pain into the work.

---

## The Withdrawal Decade (roughly 1983–1995, depowered Avengers-supporting and Lindsay-McCabe-PI period)

**Affect regulation.** Substantially improved through the simplest intervention available to her: reduction of stimulus load. Powered down, less iconic, working a profession (private investigation) that is structurally low-affect, she stabilizes. This is not therapeutic resolution — it is *symptomatic remission via environmental control*. The trauma is not processed; it is sequestered behind reduced demand.

**Cognitive style.** The investigator's discipline crystallizes here. The PI work matches her pre-existing empirical-skeptical bent and gives it a vocational structure: hypothesis, evidence, surveillance, withholding of judgment, control of information asymmetry. Critically, the work also lets her *observe intimacy without being observed in it* — she watches infidelities, family secrets, the unraveling of others' lives. This is psychologically not incidental. It is a sustained, paid practice of *being the unseen seer*, which gratifies a part of her that finds being seen unbearable.

**Self-concept.** Diminished in intensity, not improved in content. She is no longer publicly Spider-Woman; she does not have to *be* the monstrous-evolved-spider-thing in the public eye every day. The relief is real. But the underlying self-concept does not heal — it merely becomes less actively painful. This is the period in which her tolerance for loneliness deepens to clinically concerning levels. She does not feel lonely *because she has trained herself out of the affect*, which is a hollow victory.

**Attachment.** Stabilizes around Lindsay McCabe as the single secure base. The Lindsay relationship is the most important developmental fact of this decade. It is platonic, mutually professional, allows asymmetric demand, and tolerates her withdrawals — and it persists for years. This is, in attachment terms, an *earned secure* relational template laid down in adulthood, which research suggests is among the more durable psychological assets a complex-trauma survivor can acquire. Everything she does relationally in later decades draws on the template Lindsay first established.

**Defensive hierarchy.** Migration toward neurotic and the lower end of mature. *Sublimation* (work), *suppression* (deliberate non-rumination, conscious shelving of the past), and a still-heavy *intellectualization*. Acting out diminishes. The defenses are not yet mature in Vaillant's sense (no real altruism, no humor as defense yet) but they are organized.

---

## The Reactivation and Recruitment Period (roughly 2003–2008, leading into and through the Skrull captivity)

This decade is the cruelest in the file because most of its published content is not actually her. The real Jessica spent the bulk of this period in a Skrull pod undergoing repeated memory extraction and biological sampling, while Veranke walked the world wearing her face and inhabiting her relationships.

**Affect regulation during captivity (inferred).** Captivity of this duration and invasiveness produces, predictably, the full Herman complex-trauma sequence: initial protest and resistance, exhaustion, dissociative shutdown, and eventually a chronic dissociative baseline punctuated by procedural distress. The Skrull memory-harvesting would have been particularly destructive because it iteratively required her to access and surrender autobiographical material — the very mental contents on which a coherent self depends. Each harvest is, functionally, a small ego death. The subject who emerges from the pod in *Secret Invasion* #8 is not the subject who entered it; she is someone who has spent years being *taken apart and observed*, and who now must reconstruct from scratch.

**Cognitive style on emergence.** Hypervigilant, mistrust-saturated, but cognitively intact. The investigative discipline survives the captivity; if anything it sharpens, because she now has direct experiential warrant for the proposition that *appearances are unreliable to a metaphysical depth*. The world she returns to is one in which any face might not be the face — and she lived inside that proposition for years.

**Self-concept on emergence.** Annihilated and provisional. The world has been mourning, hating, or trusting an impostor wearing her face. Her friends grieve betrayals she did not commit; the public knows her through actions she did not take. There is no continuous social self to return to. She has to decide, in her thirties or forties depending on era-dating, whether to inhabit the social position the Skrull built or repudiate it — and she chooses the harder thing, which is to repudiate it without dramatizing the repudiation, simply by doing the work of being herself in the world while everyone catches up.

**Attachment.** Severed and reconstituted. The Lindsay relationship endures because Lindsay is structured for it. The relationship with Carol Danvers — which the Skrull had built — has to be re-built *as itself*, with the prior friendship usable as a template but not as a substance. Carol's choice to accept this and do that work is the second-most-important relational fact of Jessica's adult life.

**Defensive hierarchy.** Regression under load. The mature defenses being assembled in the prior decade are partially overwhelmed; isolation of affect and dissociative withdrawal return as primary mechanisms. *Counterphobic action* now becomes a stable feature — going toward the threat alone, repeatedly, as a way of asserting agency over the experience of having been a passive captive.

---

## The Hunting Years (roughly 2009–2013, post-Invasion solo work)

**Affect regulation.** Functionally impaired in a specific way: she has *stopped feeling many things in real time* and instead processes them in narrated retrospect. The second-person internal monologue characteristic of this period is a clinical sign — depersonalized self-address is a recognized dissociative marker, the subject relating to her own life as something happening to a person she is watching. She is operational; she is not integrated.

**Cognitive style.** Mission-narrowed. The hunt for residual Skrulls organizes cognition around a single object and protects her from the wider problem of what to do with herself. This is *avoidance dressed as agency* — the work is real and necessary, but it serves the additional function of postponing the reconstructive project the captivity necessitated.

**Self-concept.** Negatively organized around what she is *not* (Veranke, the Skrull, the impostor). Defining oneself by contrast to an enemy is a known precarious strategy: it borrows coherence from the antagonist, and collapses when the antagonist is defeated or absent. This is part of why the post-hunt years required another reorganization.

**Sleep architecture.** Disrupted to a degree that becomes its own clinical fact. Patrol-as-substitute-for-sleep, insomnia narrated explicitly. The chronic sleep deprivation has predictable effects on affect regulation, intrusion symptoms, and judgment — all of which the published record shows.

**Defensive hierarchy.** Heavy *displacement* (channeling unprocessable rage at the captors onto present-day targets), *isolation of affect*, persistent *intellectualization*, with sublimation continuing to do the heaviest mature-defense work.

---

## The Street-Level Reconstruction (roughly 2014–2017, Hopeless run, pregnancy and early motherhood)

This is the period of the most psychologically consequential change in the entire file.

**Affect regulation.** Pregnancy and motherhood force engagement with affect in ways that cannot be deferred. The deliberately humorous register of the Hopeless run is not cosmetic — it is *humor moving up the defensive hierarchy into the mature band*. Vaillant places humor as a mature defense precisely because it metabolizes distress in real time while remaining socially binding. The shift from the depersonalized narrator of the prior period to a wry, exasperated, embodied first-person voice is a measurable maturational event.

**Cognitive style.** Newly focused on the practical and the local. The decision to do street-level work — helping people the larger heroes overlook — is intellectually a recalibration of moral economy: the marginal utility of her competence is highest where it is least sought. This is consistent with both her empirical bent and her earned mistrust of large institutions.

**Self-concept.** Loaded onto a single new pillar: *mother of Gerry*. This provides, for the first time in her life, a continuous social role that is not derivable from the manipulation of others. She chose it, and the role's truth does not depend on anyone else's compliance. Clinically this is enormous. The vulnerability — diagnosed in the synthesis and worth re-emphasizing — is that *load-bearing single pillars are dangerous*; if anything happens to Gerry, the structural collapse will be proportionate to the pillar's centrality.

**Attachment.** *Active construction of chosen family.* The Gocking and Urich relationships are deliberate engineering. Neither is romantic; both are scaffolded around shared care for Gerry; both tolerate her work patterns. She has, by this period, learned the lesson of the Lindsay relationship and is iterating on it. This is *earned secure* attachment broadening from a single relationship to a small system. In Bowlbyian terms, she is finally building the internal working model of a world in which selected others can be trusted to remain.

**Defensive hierarchy.** The most mature configuration of her life to date. *Humor*, *sublimation* (the work as expression of care), *altruism* (street-level help as both gift and self-regulation), *suppression* (conscious choice not to ruminate). Immature defenses still recur under load but no longer dominate baseline functioning.

---

## The Current Period (roughly 2020–present, Pacheco/Perez era and after)

**Affect regulation.** The most stable in her file. The retconned-parentage revelation — that Jonathan Drew was not biologically her father — is processed with notably more equanimity than past identity disruptions. This is direct evidence of accumulated capacity. A subject who in 1980 would have experienced this revelation as catastrophic now experiences it as a difficult datum to be integrated. The mechanism is partly the diversified self-concept (she is a mother, a partner-in-care, an investigator, a fighter — not solely a Drew), and partly the rehearsed experience of surviving prior such revelations.

**Cognitive style.** Mature investigator's stance fully established. She tests, she withholds, she revises slowly but does revise, she tolerates ambiguity without anxiety. There is a quality of *patience* in the late-period writing that earlier eras lack.

**Self-concept.** Multi-pillared and provisional in a healthier sense. She holds her identity loosely now not because she is wary of investment but because she has learned, experientially, that identity-as-process survives shocks that identity-as-fixed-object cannot. This is closer to what Kegan would call a self-authoring stage — she is the author of her own meaning-making, no longer subject to it.

**Attachment.** Earned secure within the small chosen system; selectively avoidant outside it. The pattern is now *chosen* rather than reactive. She does not let in many people; the few she lets in, she lets in deeply and durably.

**Defensive hierarchy.** Predominantly mature. Humor, sublimation, altruism, suppression, anticipation (she now plans for adverse contingencies in a way the early Jessica did not). Counterphobic action remains as a residual under-stress pattern and is still her most likely route to harm. Isolation of affect and dissociative narration reappear under specific triggers (identity-attacks, threats to Gerry) but no longer organize baseline functioning.

---

## Trajectory Summary

The longitudinal arc is one of *slow defensive maturation against repeated severe insult*, in which each major reconstructive period built on the relational discoveries of the prior one: Lindsay taught her that withdrawal could be tolerated without loss; Carol taught her that a relationship could be rebuilt from the ground after the ground was destroyed; Gerry taught her that a self could be founded on care given rather than care received; the chosen family of the Hopeless period taught her that the Lindsay-template generalized. By the current period she has assembled, against considerable odds and at significant cost, something that functions as an *earned secure* adult psychological organization — fragile under specific attacks, durable under most others, and recognizably hers in a way that no earlier configuration ever quite was. The clinical interest of the case is precisely that this outcome was not predicted by the early prognosis; the developmental and adolescent picture would have justified a much worse trajectory. That she got here is a fact about her, not about the conditions, and it is the most important single datum in the file.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — JESSICA MIRIAM DREW

*File section 4 of 11. Draws on behavioral observation across published surveillance window 1977–present (≈47 years). Diagnostic framework: DSM-5-TR primary, ICD-11 where it produces meaningfully better fit, with notation of where the subject's circumstances exceed the validation envelope of either nosology (no diagnostic manual is calibrated for serial extraterrestrial captivity or chemically-mediated involuntary social aversion, and clinical humility is required.)*

---

## 4.1 Summary Statement

Subject is a 40s-range female (chronological age unreliable due to suspended-animation captivity periods) presenting with a chronic, treatment-naïve, partially-compensated **Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (ICD-11 6B41)** of approximately three decades' duration, with superimposed **acute PTSD reactivations** following each major identity-disruption event, persistent **insomnia disorder**, episodic **depersonalization/derealization** phenomena that do not meet threshold for a standalone dissociative diagnosis, and a stable **anxious-avoidant interpersonal organization** that does not rise to personality disorder. She is high-functioning, occupationally competent, capable of love and humor, parenting her child adequately and arguably well, and there is no evidence of psychotic process, mood-disorder spectrum primary illness, substance use disorder, or eating disorder. The dossier-relevant clinical fact is that her diagnosis is *less severe than her history would predict* — the gap between trauma load and current functional level is the most striking single datapoint in her psychiatric profile and demands explanation, which this section attempts.

---

## 4.2 Primary Diagnosis: Complex PTSD (ICD-11 6B41)

ICD-11's Complex PTSD construct fits Subject substantially better than DSM-5-TR's PTSD with dissociative subtype (309.81), and the reasons are diagnostically instructive.

### 4.2.1 Criterion A — Stressor

Subject's qualifying stressor history is **prolonged, repeated, identity-targeted, and inflicted by figures of trust or pseudo-trust** — the ICD-11 C-PTSD prototype. Inventory:

- **Developmental (ages ~5–14):** isolation on Wundagore Mountain among non-human peers; experimental somatic interventions by the paternal figure; absence of normative human peer socialization through latency and early adolescence. This is not classical Criterion A in DSM-5-TR terms (no overt threat to life) but constitutes **chronic developmental adversity** under any reasonable trauma-informed reading and is the substrate on which everything subsequent has compounded.
- **Adolescent (ages ~15–early 20s):** HYDRA recruitment by Otto Vermis under conditions meeting modern criteria for **cult-style coercive control** — sleep manipulation, identity reprogramming (the "you are an evolved spider" cover story), trained dissociation under combat conditions, instrumental seduction. Rupture event: belief that she had killed Jerry Hunt, an attachment figure inside the system. This is the first of her **betrayal-trauma** events (Freyd's framework applies cleanly: harm inflicted by a figure on whom survival/attachment depends).
- **Adult, repeated:** romantic and operational betrayals across the Wolfman/Claremont era; the **Skrull captivity** (multi-year confinement, invasive procedures, memory extraction — meets every Criterion A subcriterion DSM-5-TR enumerates and several it does not contemplate); the post-recovery social trauma of returning to a world where an enemy had been wearing her face and her closest associates had not noticed; the **retconned-parentage** revelation (an identity-attack delivered as information rather than violence, but nevertheless threat-coded for her specifically).

The cumulative profile is a textbook ICD-11 stressor: prolonged, inescapable, with the perpetrator class repeatedly being *those who were supposed to protect or know her*.

### 4.2.2 Core PTSD Cluster — Present

- **Re-experiencing:** Nightmares (well-documented post-*Secret Invasion*), intrusive imagery cued by HYDRA insignia, Skrull morphology, and certain interrogation-room geometries. She does not typically report intrusions verbally — they manifest as sudden tactical withdrawal mid-conversation, brief affective flattening, or the trademark second-person internal narration that her writers render as caption text and which is, clinically, a **dissociative re-experiencing variant** — she is observing the present moment from outside it because the present has cued a past in which being inside her own body was unsafe.
- **Avoidance:** Geographic (her repeated relocations — London, Los Angeles, San Francisco, Madripoor — track loosely with proximity to trauma cues); relational (rationing of intimate contact); cognitive (she will discuss the Skrull captivity *operationally* but resists processing it *affectively*; this is functional avoidance in a person whose work requires the operational frame).
- **Hyperarousal / hypervigilance:** Insomnia, exaggerated startle (modulated by training but observable in unguarded moments), constant scanning behavior in public space, defensive seating choices (backs to walls, exits in sight — see Section 7, Behavioral Micro-Patterns).
- **Negative cognitions and mood:** Persistent low-grade dysphoria, sense of foreshortened future during acute periods, belief that intimacy is unsafe-by-default, periodic statements consistent with survivor guilt regarding those harmed by her Skrull impostor.

### 4.2.3 Complex PTSD-Specific Clusters — Present

ICD-11 requires three additional clusters beyond core PTSD to diagnose C-PTSD. Subject meets all three.

- **Disturbances in self-organization — affect dysregulation.** Her difficulty is not lability; it is *narrow-band dysregulation specific to anger*. She over-regulates anger in real time (cold, controlled, surgical violence rather than outburst) but has **difficulty terminating the activated state once it is engaged**. The post-Invasion hunting arc is the cleanest behavioral evidence: an anger that does not extinguish on schedule, that pursues past the operational point at which a less-injured operator would stand down. Fear, sadness, and shame she regulates well — almost too well — likely through habitual suppression that costs her elsewhere.
- **Negative self-concept.** Persistent across the full 47-year record: descriptions of herself as monstrous, alien, contaminated, "made wrong," not-quite-human. Pre-dates any single trauma; was cemented in adolescence; has been *modulated* but never eliminated by adult achievement. She has never spontaneously described herself in positive terms without qualifying immediately.
- **Disturbances in relationships.** Avoidant attachment with selective deep bonds (see Section 5, Personality); pattern of withdrawal under intimacy pressure; difficulty asking for help; difficulty believing she is wanted rather than tolerated. Stable when established, but the *establishment cost* is high and getting higher with each betrayal.

### 4.2.4 Why C-PTSD and not classical PTSD with dissociative subtype

DSM-5-TR's dissociative-subtype PTSD captures the depersonalization and derealization but **does not capture the negative self-concept or the interpersonal disturbance as diagnostic features** — it treats them as associated. For Subject these are not associated, they are *central*; they predate the indexable acute traumas; and they organize her clinical picture more than the re-experiencing does. ICD-11's C-PTSD construct makes them criterial, which is the correct level of weight. If the assessor is restricted to DSM-5-TR, the appropriate formulation is PTSD with dissociative subtype **plus** a careful Z-code annotation of the developmental history and interpersonal pattern; this is a nosological workaround, not a substantive difference.

---

## 4.3 Secondary / Concurrent Diagnoses

### 4.3.1 Insomnia Disorder (DSM-5-TR 780.52 / ICD-11 7A00)

Independent of PTSD-attributable sleep disturbance, Subject meets criteria for chronic insomnia disorder: difficulty initiating and maintaining sleep, ≥3 nights/week, ≥3 months, with daytime consequences (though her superhuman physiology absorbs more sleep deprivation than a baseline human, behavioral markers of fatigue — judgment compression, terseness, micro-irritability — appear after sustained deprivation). She has weaponized the insomnia into productivity (nighttime patrol, surveillance, PI casework). This is **functionalized symptom expression** and is common in high-performing trauma survivors; it stabilizes the system but forecloses recovery.

### 4.3.2 Depersonalization/Derealization phenomena, subthreshold

Episodic; trauma-cued; transient; does not meet duration/distress criteria for Depersonalization/Derealization Disorder (DSM-5-TR 300.6). Best classified as a dissociative feature of her C-PTSD rather than a standalone diagnosis. The literal soul-body separation in early canon (*Spider-Woman* #50) is a **metaphysical event within the universe, not a symptom**, and must not be folded into the diagnostic picture — though it may have *retraumatized* her dissociative substrate.

### 4.3.3 Adjustment reactions, recurrent

Each major identity-disruption event (Skrull recovery, retconned parentage, Gerry's birth, each major team dissolution) has produced a discrete period of impaired functioning lasting weeks to months, with affective and behavioral features. These are **adjustment disorders superimposed on a C-PTSD substrate** — diagnostically distinct because they remit when the precipitating stressor's salience decays. The Hopeless-era pregnancy adjustment is the only one that resolved with *positive* re-stabilization rather than mere symptom decay.

### 4.3.4 Reproductive / postpartum considerations

No documented postpartum depression or postpartum psychosis. Risk factors were high (trauma history, irregular obstetric circumstances, single parenting). Protective factors that prevented expected morbidity: deliberate scaffolding by Carol Danvers, the chosen-family configuration with Roger Gocking and Ben Urich, and what appears to be a genuine reorganization of meaning around the maternal role. This is **clinically significant resilience** and should be cataloged as such rather than assumed.

---

## 4.4 Etiology — Layered Model

A clean formulation requires distinguishing the **etiological strata**, because intervention at the wrong layer would fail.

1. **Constitutional substrate.** Non-human physiology; involuntary pheromone secretion producing chemically-mediated social aversion from female humans and unreliable attraction signal from male humans. This is not a psychiatric etiology in itself but is a **lifelong social-environmental insult** that has shaped every subsequent layer. No baseline-human comparison case exists in the literature.
2. **Developmental.** Wundagore isolation; absence of normative peer attachment; experimental somatic procedures inflicted by paternal figure; primary attachment to non-human caregiver (Bova). Result: **insecure attachment template** with an organizational defect — the developmental experience of "human" is itself partially absent, so her sense of belonging to the species is provisional.
3. **Adolescent indoctrination.** HYDRA coercive control. Result: **second-layer attachment trauma** plus the specific cognitive imprint that *systems that offer belonging are weapons*. This is the layer responsible for her institutional skepticism.
4. **Adult repeated trauma.** Captivity, identity-theft, betrayal, combat exposure. Result: **PTSD/C-PTSD symptom load** in the classical sense, layered on the prior two strata.
5. **Iatrogenic / retroactive.** Each retconned origin functions, from her phenomenological standpoint, as a fresh assault on autobiographical continuity. This is a category of trauma the diagnostic manuals do not contemplate but which is **clinically real for her**: the periodic discovery that her own history was not what she believed is, subjectively, indistinguishable from gaslighting on a cosmic scale. The accumulated effect is **autobiographical-memory mistrust** — she now holds her own narrative loosely as a defense against the next revision.

Any treatment plan that addressed only layer 4 would relapse her on layer 3 cues; any that addressed only layers 3–4 would leave the constitutional and developmental substrates exposed. The good news is that the C-PTSD formulation is broad enough to organize all layers under one rubric.

---

## 4.5 Symptom Presentation in Observable Behavior

The diagnostic features map to observable behavior as follows, for surveillance-correlation purposes:

- **Re-experiencing →** mid-conversation micro-disengagements (3–8 seconds, eyes unfocused, returns with a deflective remark); nightmares evidenced by next-day pattern of pre-dawn patrol logs; resistance to certain mission profiles articulated as tactical objection but timed to trauma-cue proximity.
- **Avoidance →** geographic relocations following major stress events; declining of social invitations clustered around anniversaries (the Vermis rupture, the Skrull recovery date); abrupt topic changes when conversation approaches her childhood.
- **Hyperarousal →** seating choices (always with sightline to entry); insomnia activity (patrol, casework, gym); near-total absence of relaxation behaviors in unobserved time; tonic muscular guarding in shoulders and jaw visible in still imagery.
- **Affect dysregulation (anger) →** post-engagement perseveration — she will continue investigating a closed threat for days past tactical necessity; difficulty disengaging from a hunt; in the Skrull-pursuit period, observable extension of operational tempo beyond what colleagues judged necessary.
- **Negative self-concept →** self-deprecating humor as a near-tic; consistent refusal of compliments; pattern of describing accomplishments in third-person operational terms ("the job got done") rather than first-person credit-claiming.
- **Interpersonal disturbance →** rationed contact with even close associates; long silences between communications with people she demonstrably loves; resistance to receiving care; readiness to provide care.
- **Dissociative features →** the second-person internal voice; brief depersonalization episodes under acute stress; **NOT** identity alteration, **NOT** time loss in any clinically meaningful sense.

---

## 4.6 Course Over Time

- **1977–1983 (Wolfman/Claremont era):** Acute and unmanaged. Symptom load high, supports thin, functioning by force. Repeated relational failures. Identity unstable.
- **1983–2000s (dormant period):** **Spontaneous partial remission via reduced exposure.** Depowering removed her from the trauma-generating environment. The PI work and Lindsay McCabe relationship constituted, in effect, an **unstructured naturalistic exposure-and-stabilization period.** This is the only sustained interval of relative health in her record, and its features (steady non-romantic intimate friendship, lower-stakes work, geographic stability) should be cataloged as her demonstrated stabilization profile.
- **Mid-2000s Bendis era → Secret Invasion:** **Catastrophic relapse and acute trauma deposition.** Captivity period is the single worst psychiatric event in her file.
- **Post-Invasion (2009–2010):** **Acute C-PTSD presentation, undertreated** (treatment not sought; self-managed through revenge-coded activity). The motion-comic narration is essentially a clinical record of derealization.
- **Hopeless era (2014–2017):** **Active reconstruction.** Motherhood reorganizes meaning; chosen family scaffolds attachment repair; street-level work provides values-congruent occupation. **Best-functioning period since the early-1990s PI work and arguably ever.**
- **Pacheco/Perez era (2020–present):** **Accrued resilience visible.** Processes the retconned-parentage revelation with notably less destabilization than past identity-attacks. She has internalized that her selfhood is *constructed and durable*, not *given and fragile*. This is genuine clinical progress, unaided by formal treatment, which speaks to her constitutional resilience and the protective value of her current supports.

**Prognosis:** Guarded-favorable. The longitudinal trajectory is improving despite continued trauma exposure. The single largest current risk factor is the **load-bearing nature of the Gerry-as-identity-anchor**: should harm come to her son, the architecture of her current stability would not hold. Secondary risk: another identity-attack of sufficient novelty to bypass her accrued defenses. Tertiary risk: the cumulative cost of chronic sleep restriction.

---

## 4.7 Differential Diagnosis — What She Is Not, and Why

Rigorous differential is critical here because surface features of Subject's presentation invite several incorrect framings, each of which would distort intervention and surveillance interpretation.

### 4.7.1 NOT Borderline Personality Disorder

Surface invitation: identity disturbance, intense relationships, history of trauma, anger regulation difficulty.

Why ruled out:
- **No abandonment panic.** BPD's frantic-efforts-to-avoid-abandonment criterion is conspicuously absent; she more often *initiates* withdrawal than fears it.
- **No splitting.** Her appraisals of others are stable, nuanced, and slow to revise — the opposite of BPD's idealization/devaluation oscillation.
- **No impulsivity in self-damaging domains.** No sexual impulsivity, no spending, no substance use, no binge eating, no reckless driving outside of mission context (and in-mission risk-taking is calibrated, not impulsive).
- **No chronic emptiness in the BPD sense.** Her dysphoria is *populated* — by memory, by responsibility, by anger — not empty.
- **Identity disturbance is externally inflicted and reality-based**, not endogenous and shifting. A Skrull literally wore her face. A revised origin was published. These are not BPD identity diffusion; they are external assaults on a self that, between assaults, holds steady.
- **Relationships, once established, are durable.** BPD relationships are stormy; hers are quiet and lasting.

### 4.7.2 NOT Schizoid Personality Disorder

Surface invitation: social distance, solitary work, restricted affective expression in public.

Why ruled out:
- **She desires close relationships and grieves their absence.** SPD individuals are *indifferent* to closeness; she is *defended against* it. The distinction is criterial and clinically obvious in her case: she sustains decades-long deep bonds (Lindsay, Carol) and forms new ones (Roger, Ben). A schizoid individual would not.
- **Affective range, in close company, is full and warm.** The flatness is contextual, not constitutional.
- **Pleasure in activities is preserved.** Schizoid anhedonia is absent.

### 4.7.3 NOT Schizotypal Personality Disorder

Surface invitation: unusual experiences (the dissociative phenomena, the soul-body separation), constricted affect, social anxiety.

Why ruled out:
- **No magical thinking, ideas of reference, or odd beliefs.** Her cognitive style is **empirical to the point of severity** — the opposite of schizotypal. The "unusual experiences" in her history are not subjective oddities; they are objective in-universe events (genuine soul separation, genuine alien replacement), and her interpretation of them is uniformly grounded.
- **No perceptual disturbances outside trauma-cued dissociation.**

### 4.7.4 NOT Antisocial Personality Disorder, despite assassin training

Surface invitation: trained killer, capable of cold violence, history of deception (PI work, infiltration).

Why ruled out:
- **Conscience is intact and overactive.** Her killings haunt her; her deceptions distress her; she rejects the HYDRA frame in her teens precisely because she could not tolerate what she had done.
- **No childhood conduct disorder pattern.**
- **No exploitative interpersonal style.** She declines to use her pheromones manipulatively even when it would advantage her.

### 4.7.5 NOT Major Depressive Disorder as primary

Surface invitation: chronic dysphoria, sleep disturbance, social withdrawal, negative self-concept.

Why ruled out:
- **Baseline is dysphoric-functional, not anhedonic.** She experiences pleasure (in her son, in competence, in friendship, in dark humor) reliably.
- **Episodic depressive periods are post-trauma reactive**, time-limited, and remit with environmental change or active reconstruction — consistent with adjustment reactions or PTSD-attributable mood disturbance, not primary unipolar depression.
- **No psychomotor signature of MDD.** Energy is mobilized, not depleted.
- That said: she meets enough threshold features that a **screening evaluation for MDD should be repeated at each major life transition.** The risk is real, just not currently realized.

### 4.7.6 NOT Bipolar Spectrum

No history of hypomanic or manic episodes. Periods of intense activity are **goal-directed and proportional to threat**, not energized-elevated-grandiose. Sleep reduction is **stressor-driven and ego-dystonic**, not part of an elevated state. No cyclicity.

### 4.7.7 NOT Dissociative Identity Disorder

Surface invitation: literal soul-body separation in canon, literal Skrull replacement, the second-person voice, history of indoctrination.

Why ruled out — and this matters because it would be the easy misread:
- **One continuous sense of self across the entire record.** No alter system; no identified self-states with distinct names/ages/preferences; no inter-state amnesia in the clinical sense.
- **The Skrull replacement was not a dissociative event for her** — she was held elsewhere during it. It was an event done *to* her social field while she was absent. This is identity *theft*, not identity *fragmentation*.
- **The HYDRA-conditioned identity was a single overlaid false narrative**, not a dissociative compartment, and it resolved into integration rather than alternation.
- **The depersonalization and derealization episodes are PTSD-spectrum, not DID-spectrum**: she observes her continuous self from outside, rather than becoming a different self.

### 4.7.8 NOT a Psychotic-Spectrum Disorder

No hallucinations attributable to her own brain; no delusions; no formal thought disorder; reality-testing is intact and arguably superior to baseline (she has been calibrated by repeated experience of having reality be stranger than reported). The unusual content of her experience is **environmental, not generated.**

### 4.7.9 NOT Substance Use Disorder

Despite a trauma load that statistically predicts substance use, she has none. Social drinking is moderate. No self-medication pattern. This is **notable resilience** and likely reflects: (a) her physiology metabolizes intoxicants atypically, reducing reinforcement; (b) her behavioral substitutes (work, combat, patrol) occupy


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS: JESSICA DREW

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, 1977–present. Cross-referenced against subject's own statements, third-party testimony (Danvers, McCabe, Gocking, Cage, Barton), and direct surveillance product. Tells are organized by condition state, then by channel (somatic, kinesic, paralinguistic, linguistic, tactical, environmental). What follows is the granular record. Take it as evidence, not as caricature.*

---

## I. BASELINE / CALM STATE

The subject's true calm is rare and observable for what it is precisely because she does not perform it. When Jessica Drew is genuinely at ease — privately, in low-stakes domestic interludes, in the hour after putting Gerry to sleep — her body settles into a posture that no surveillance file before motherhood ever captured: shoulders down rather than rolled forward, jaw unclenched, the small habitual tension she carries in the right trapezius visibly absent. This baseline lasts in fifteen-to-forty-minute windows and is the only condition under which her resting respiration drops below approximately fourteen breaths per minute.

**Somatic.** Sits asymmetrically — one leg drawn up, the other planted — almost never both feet on the floor unless in a professional posture she is consciously holding. Carries weight on the left hip when standing; favors the right hand for fine work and the left for grip. Touches her own forearms when reading — left fingertips on right wrist, a self-soothing tell that predates the Skrull captivity and intensified after. Wears her hair down only when alone or with Lindsay; tied back, with a single elastic kept on her right wrist as a backup, in every operational context for forty-plus years.

**Kinesic.** Slow blink rate. Eyes scan the room on entry — corners first, exits second, occupants third — but in calm state the scan is single-pass and unrepeated. She will sit with her back to a door only in three documented environments: Lindsay McCabe's apartment, Carol Danvers's kitchen, and her own son's bedroom. This is the single cleanest trust-instrument in the file.

**Paralinguistic.** Voice drops about a third of an octave from her professional register. Speech tempo slows. Uses contractions she suppresses in court testimony and in formal Avengers contexts. Laughs audibly — a low, slightly hoarse laugh that does not appear in any HYDRA-era footage and is, by her own offhand admission, something she had to relearn.

**Linguistic.** Speaks in the first person. (The shift to first person is the single best indicator that she is regulated; persistent second-person internal narration is a flag we treat as clinical.) Asks open questions. Volunteers small autobiographical fragments — childhood Wundagore details, mostly comic, mostly about Bova — that she will not share in any other state.

**Habits and rituals.** Coffee black, two cups before speaking to anyone except Gerry. Reads a physical book (genre fiction, often paperback noir or astronomy nonfiction) before sleep when sleep is available. Cooks rarely but well; has a small repertoire of about six dishes she rotates, all one-pan, all developed during the London years and Los Angeles PI period when kitchen space was minimal. Pays in cash for small purchases when not operational. Keeps the apartment cold (≈ 64°F) and the lights low.

---

## II. MILD STRESS / LOW-GRADE PROFESSIONAL FRICTION

This is the dominant state — her *working* state. Decades of operational tempo have shaped a stress baseline most subjects would clinically classify as activation; for her it is room temperature.

**Somatic.** Trapezius tension returns within minutes of an inbound problem. Jaw locks subtly — visible as a small recurring flex at the masseter. Bites the inside of her lower lip during phone calls; the inner mucosa shows the chronic mark. Cracks the knuckles of her left hand against the heel of her right palm, never the reverse. Stands more often than sits.

**Kinesic.** Door-scan becomes recurrent — every four to six minutes, the eyes recheck exits without her registering she is doing it. Begins to mirror conversation partners less; the mirroring she does in calm state shuts off as a measure of cognitive load redirection.

**Paralinguistic.** Voice rises back to its professional register. Sentences shorten. Filler words ("um," "you know") drop almost entirely — under load she becomes more articulate, not less, which is the opposite of the population baseline and itself a tell.

**Linguistic.** Dry humor sharpens to the point of being a recognizable signature. Uses humor as a probe — she will joke about the situation to see who flinches, who laughs, who is too task-focused to notice. The flinchers get filed; the laughers get marginal trust; the non-noticers get watched. She becomes terser, more declarative. The captioned interior monologue (when she narrates her own life, which she does silently and almost constantly) shifts from past to present tense.

**Decision habits.** Triages by *who is in the room she can rely on*. Will accept tactical command if no one better is present and will hand it off the instant someone competent appears. Tends to take the on-the-ground role rather than the coordinating one. Defers strategic planning to consultation partners she trusts (Danvers; in earlier eras, Cage and Cap) and rarely contests their reads — *unless* the plan requires her to trust someone she has not vetted, at which point she will quietly substitute her own plan and execute it.

**Environmental.** Begins to position herself relative to exits and to civilians. Keeps her phone in the right hand or in a pocket from which it can be drawn one-handed. Eats less; will skip a meal without noticing.

---

## III. MODERATE STRESS / OPERATIONAL UNCERTAINTY

The threshold-crossing here is the activation of *compartmentalization as active behavior* rather than passive structure. She begins, audibly and physically, to put parts of her life into boxes and shut the lids.

**Somatic.** Sleep collapses first. She will work through one night, then a second; by the third the skin under her eyes thins to a visible discoloration she does not concealer-cover (a small datum: her vanity is highly selective and operates almost exclusively in social-civilian contexts). Appetite suppression deepens. She loses two to four pounds within a week of any sustained operation; muscle preserves, fat depletes. Caffeine intake roughly doubles.

**Kinesic.** Stillness increases. Where calm-state Jessica fidgets in small ways, moderate-stress Jessica freezes the small motor activity entirely — a held quality, as if conserving for the larger movement she expects to need. She crosses her arms more, but low — at the diaphragm, not the chest — which is a self-containment posture rather than a defensive one.

**Paralinguistic.** Speech becomes clipped. The hoarse register she has when fully calm goes thin and clean. She stops laughing audibly. The sardonic edge in her speech sharpens until it can cut.

**Linguistic.** Begins to use the second person on herself, silently — *you don't have time for this; you check the perimeter; you don't sleep yet* — which we know about because she has bled it into spoken English in front of trusted observers (notably Danvers, who has reported it without naming it). This is the single most diagnostically important behavioral marker in the entire file. Persistent second-person self-address is the threshold at which her dissociative defenses are active and load-bearing.

**Decision habits.** Reduces consultation, not increases it. The instinct under moderate stress is to *handle it before involving anyone* — a learned behavior from the HYDRA, post-HYDRA, and post-Skrull eras when reaching out had been punished or had been received by an enemy wearing a friend's face. She will text Carol Danvers updates rather than questions. She will tell Roger Gocking she has it handled. She will not call Lindsay at all, which is a partial protection — Lindsay is the relationship she most insulates from operational ugliness.

**Environmental.** Walks more, drives less. Foot patrol routes (see Section VII below) intensify. Pays cash exclusively. Phone gets put on airplane mode for stretches.

---

## IV. THREAT / ACTIVE HOSTILE CONDITIONS

Here the behavioral picture inverts from what civilians expect of a frightened person. The subject does not flinch outward; she focuses inward and then moves *toward*.

**Somatic.** Pupils dilate noticeably; breathing slows rather than quickens (a trained inhibition, present in her work from the Wolfman run forward). Skin temperature drops at the extremities — fingers cool — as peripheral vasoconstriction kicks in. Pheromone output appears to spike under threat, which she cannot prevent and which we have observed her use deliberately when no other option is available; this is not a comfortable adaptation for her and it costs her something psychologically each time.

**Kinesic.** Goes still. Becomes economical in a way that is itself signature — a person who has fought in many bodies and has stripped away every motion that is not necessary. Drops the asymmetric weight distribution of her calm posture and grounds evenly. Hands open by default rather than closed; she does not telegraph the venom blast.

**Paralinguistic.** Voice drops, considerably and deliberately, into a low controlled register. Does not raise volume. Cadence becomes metronomic. She will give one warning, usually, in a tone that has caused trained operatives to comply.

**Linguistic.** Speech reduces to the operational minimum. Will use names — the target's, her ally's, the hostage's — as anchoring tools, both for the listener and for herself. Sarcasm disappears under genuine threat; sarcasm is a *moderate*-stress tool, not a high-stress one.

**Decision habits.** *Counterphobic engagement.* This is the most documented behavioral pattern in her file and the most consistent across eras. When threatened, she goes toward the threat. When isolated, she presses isolation further (will refuse extraction if extraction would expose others). When given the choice between waiting for backup and proceeding alone, she will proceed alone *if she judges the threat to be one only she can metabolize* — and her judgment of this is reliably skewed toward *yes*. She has been killed and resurrected and depowered and replaced and she still steps forward.

**Failure mode.** *Isolated overcompetence.* She will burn herself to the wick before she will ask. She will under-report injury — broken ribs treated as bruising, concussions worked through, the captivity-era muscle wasting hidden under loose layers — because asking has historically been punished by the asker being made into someone else's tool. The file should mark this clearly: in any threat condition, *her self-report of her own status is unreliable downward*. She will say "I'm fine" with a pneumothorax.

**Anger sub-state.** When anger activates within threat, the presentation does not change visibly — and that is the point. Her anger expresses as cold sustained violence, not outburst. She will continue past the point at which the threat is neutralized if not stopped. Documented across the post-*Secret Invasion* Skrull-hunting period: she would finish them after they had surrendered. She knows this about herself and has installed Carol Danvers as a partial brake; she will sometimes call Danvers specifically to be told to stop.

---

## V. INTIMACY (PHYSICAL AND EMOTIONAL)

This is the condition with the *largest gap* between what an external observer expects and what surveillance product records. Jessica is, in close quarters, more present and more humorous than her professional persona suggests — and almost never with more than one person at a time.

**Somatic.** Touches more in private than in public. With Lindsay, will sit close enough to brush; with Carol, will grip a forearm to make a point. With Gerry, is physically demonstrative in a way no other context produces — carries him longer than necessary, holds his hand when walking even past the age children typically reject it, sleeps with the door open. With romantic partners (historically Hunt, Magnus, Hauptmann, and the rotating short-term entanglements of the LA years and after), she initiates physical contact more often than she initiates emotional disclosure; the inversion is itself a defense.

**Kinesic.** Lowers eyes briefly when complimented sincerely and looks back up with a small wry half-smile — a tell that has been consistent since the Wolfman run. Cannot accept compliments cleanly; will either deflect with humor or absorb in silence. Does not perform vulnerability. When she is genuinely vulnerable, the signal is *less* expressive, not more: she goes quiet and still and looks at the floor middle-distance.

**Paralinguistic.** Voice softens further than even calm-state baseline — drops to something close to a murmur. Laughs more, including at her own remarks, which she will not do in any other context.

**Linguistic.** Discloses biographical detail in small controlled increments. Will tell a Wundagore story to a new intimate as a sounding — if it lands with curiosity rather than pity, more will follow; if pity, the channel closes and does not reopen for weeks. Pity is the response she punishes hardest, because pity is the response that confirms the worldview she is trying to escape.

**Decision habits.** Rations proximity. The pattern is a documented oscillation: a period of closeness, then a period of distance, then a return. The distance is not test or punishment but *recovery from exposure*. Partners who tolerate the oscillation without protest get permanence; partners who demand explanation get the door, eventually, politely. Lindsay McCabe, Carol Danvers, and Roger Gocking have all passed this filter. Most others have not.

**Sexual behavior, what we can infer.** Selective. Periods of celibacy alternating with periods of relative activity, with the activity periods coinciding with operational lulls — sex as one of the things she does when not working, not as something work interrupts. The pheromone problem means she cannot fully trust the attraction of partners; she has compensated by preferring partners who knew her *before* attraction was a factor or whose response to her predates the pheromone effect's salience. This is a small set.

**The intimacy paradox.** She wants to be known. She structures her life to make being known difficult. She is aware of the paradox. She has not resolved it; she has built workarounds.

---

## VI. GRIEF

She does not grieve quickly and she does not grieve publicly. The processing happens on a delay measured in weeks.

**Acute phase (hours to days post-loss).** Operational. Will attend to logistics — bodies, paperwork, the welfare of others affected — with a steady competence that has been mistaken for coldness by people who do not know her. Eats less, sleeps less, talks less. The voice flattens; the humor disappears entirely. Will accept embraces but will not initiate them. Will not cry in front of more than one person, and that person is almost always Lindsay or Carol.

**Subacute phase (days to weeks).** Withdrawal. Geographic if possible — has historically left the city, the country, the planet, when able. Patrol intensifies in a directionless way; she walks without purpose, sometimes for hours, in routes that wander outside her usual surveillance grid. Drinks moderately, never to intoxication. Reads more. Sleeps in unfamiliar postures — on couches, in chairs, on the floor next to Gerry's bed — as if the bed itself has become associated with thought she does not want.

**Chronic phase (weeks to months).** Returns to function without announcement. Will reference the lost person in passing, casually, as if testing whether the world can hold the reference; if it can, will reference them again. Does not perform mourning. Does not hold ritual anniversaries openly, though she observes them privately — Jerry Hunt's name has surfaced in her interior monologue in operationally documented contexts decades after his death.

**Atypical sub-pattern.** When the grief is for someone she also feels guilty toward (Hunt; the friends who grieved an impostor while she was in a Skrull pod; the relationships she could not maintain because she was replaced), the chronic phase is longer and the second-person internal narration persists further into it. Guilt-grief is the form she handles worst.

---

## VII. ROUTINES, ROUTES, AND RITUALS

The granular surveillance product:

- **Morning.** Wakes early, typically before Gerry. Forty-five minutes of solitude before the household activates — coffee, window-stand, scanning the street below. (She lives in residences with windows that look down on access points; this is a consistent housing preference across forty years.) Stretches but does not formally exercise; her conditioning is maintained by patrol.
- **Patrol patterns.** Three documented foot-route templates, rotated unpredictably: a long perimeter sweep (90+ minutes, broader than necessary, used when she needs to think), a short hot-zone loop (40 minutes, used in active operations), and a wandering route (no fixed length, used in grief and acute stress). She varies the start point and direction. She does not patrol the same route two nights in succession.
