Her counter-pattern is itself a pattern — she rotates through roughly five base templates, each modified by weather, mood, and Gerry's schedule. A patient observer over six weeks can recover the templates.
- **Safe houses and fallbacks** are kept in cash-only arrangements, often through Lindsay or Roger as intermediaries, never in her name. She maintains at least one fallback she has not told anyone about, on principle.
- **Communications** — she prefers asynchronous, brief, plain-text. Voice calls register as urgency and she answers them; video calls she dislikes and avoids. She will not discuss operations on any channel she did not personally vet.
- **Routine pleasures** — coffee from one specific neighborhood place; a small number of bars she rotates through, never the same one twice in a week; a long-standing habit of late-night walks alone that she has had to modify since Gerry but has not given up.

### VI.C. Tells

Reliable behavioral indicators across decades of canon:

- **Hand to the back of the neck**, briefly, when she is suppressing pheromone output in a tense room.
- **Slight tilt of the head, eyes unfocused for a beat** when she is consciously checking whether a memory is hers or implanted. This was rare pre-Invasion and became habitual after.
- **Dry one-liner immediately after a near-miss.** The faster and drier the joke, the closer the call was. Silence after a near-miss is the bad sign.
- **Switching to second person in her own narration** — internal, but it surfaces sometimes as her referring to herself in the second person aloud to Gerry or to herself when alone. This is the dissociation tell.
- **Standing rather than sitting in unfamiliar rooms**, even when invited to sit. She sits when she has decided the room is safe; until then she remains weight-forward.
- **Refusing to remove her jacket.** Same signal. Jacket off is a vulnerability concession.
- **Asking a question she already knows the answer to.** This is her testing whether the person will lie. Lying to her at this moment is a relationship-ending event whose end the other party will not learn about for some time.

### VI.D. What she will do under stated conditions

- **If she is asked to join a team she does not trust:** decline, observe at distance, intervene if necessary on her own terms.
- **If she is asked to choose between two of her people:** she will refuse the frame and attempt a third option, expending herself to make it real.
- **If she discovers she has been deceived by an ally:** silent withdrawal, full information audit, and a single conversation in which the ally will be given one chance to account. The conversation is not an emotional event; it is a forensic one.
- **If she discovers she has been deceived about herself:** longer processing, no immediate action, eventual integration. Post-2020 she has become measurably better at this.
- **If Gerry is threatened:** all available force, no negotiation, no quarter, and a willingness to absorb damage that would be irrational under any other condition.

---

## VII. HOW TO DESTABILIZE HER

*This section exists so that the moves catalogued here can be recognized when an adversary makes them, and countered before they complete.*

### VII.A. The four-stroke destabilization

A sophisticated adversary aiming to break her would not attack her directly. The pattern that would work, derived from the structure of her defenses, is:

1. **Isolate the chosen family.** Not eliminate — *isolate*. Move Lindsay out of the country on a plausible case. Tie Carol up in a cosmic event. Embroil Roger in a legal problem that consumes his attention. Each, individually, is unsuspicious; together they remove her social scaffolding.
2. **Introduce a small, plausible, recurring identity-doubt.** A memory that doesn't quite fit. A photograph from a period she doesn't remember being photographed. Nothing she can act on, nothing she can verify, nothing she can dismiss. Let it sit.
3. **Disrupt sleep.** Ambient, deniable, environmental. Construction noise, a new neighbor, a recurring false alarm. Drive the average below five hours for three weeks.
4. **Present a Gerry-stressor that is real but non-acute** — a school problem, a health scare, a custodial complication. Force her into the compartment she most defends, at the moment her other defenses are degraded.

At this point her counterphobic action defense will activate against the wrong target, her judgment will be impaired, and she will burn herself out attempting to solve a problem that has been designed not to be solvable by her alone.

The countermeasure is to recognize the *combination* — any two of these in the same quarter should be treated as potentially adversarial regardless of how innocuous each looks alone — and to refuse to let her solve it in isolation, which will require force, because she will resist.

### VII.B. Specific destabilization vectors, in order of severity

1. **Convincing impersonation of Gerry, sustained over time.** Catastrophic. Recovery uncertain.
2. **Demonstration that a current trusted intimate is, and has always been, an agent.** Catastrophic to her capacity to form future trust; she has the experience to survive the event but not without permanent narrowing.
3. **Public reveal that an action she took, in good faith, was actually a handler's operation.** Severe. Reactivates HYDRA-era guilt.
4. **Mind-control event of any duration.** Severe and specifically targeted at her oldest wound. Her current defenses include verification rituals with Carol and Roger; these can be defeated by a sufficiently informed adversary.
5. **Loss of the Gerry compartment's integrity** — anything that forces her superhero life and her motherhood into the same room at the same time on someone else's terms. The compartments are load-bearing; their failure does not produce collapse but produces a brittle, dangerous overcompetence.
6. **Loss of Lindsay.** Of her adult relationships, this is the longest-running and most foundational. Lindsay's death or betrayal would be a single-point structural failure.
7. **Loss of Carol.** Severe but more survivable; the relationship is reciprocal in a way the Lindsay relationship is asymmetric, and grief would be acute but processable.
8. **Forced public unmasking, particularly tying her domestic address to her costumed identity.** Operationally severe; psychologically she would adapt.

### VII.C. What does NOT destabilize her, despite appearances

- Physical injury, even severe. She has a high pain tolerance and treats injury as logistics.
- Capture, if she expects rescue is not coming. She handles solitary captivity unusually well; the Skrull experience, paradoxically, calibrated her to it.
- Public criticism, hostile press, official censure. She has been called a monster by professionals; amateurs do not reach her.
- Romantic rejection from a new partner. She expects it and metabolizes it quickly.
- Defeat in single combat. She loses fights, learns, returns.

The distinction between what destabilizes her and what does not is consistent: **threats to who she is and who is hers will break her; threats to her body, her reputation, or her plans will not.**

---

## VIII. PROTECTIVE PROTOCOLS

For anyone tasked with her wellbeing rather than her management:

1. **Maintain awareness of the chosen-family scaffold.** If Lindsay, Carol, Roger, or Ben Urich becomes unreachable for non-obvious reasons, treat as a potential indicator. Do not tell her you are watching; do tell her if you find something.
2. **Sleep, patrol, solitude, Gerry-time** are the four homeostatic variables. Track them informally. Two consecutively degraded is yellow; three is red.
3. **Verify her, gently, when you have not seen her in a while.** A small shared reference no impostor would know. Do this as habit so it does not become accusation. She will appreciate it.
4. **Do not try to fix her.** She is not broken in a way fixable from outside. She is carrying something heavy and has built a life around carrying it. Help with the carrying; do not propose she set it down.
5. **If she withdraws, let her.** Withdrawal is her primary self-regulation. Forced re-engagement is experienced as handling, which is the worst available frame. Leave the door open and unmentioned.
6. **Protect Gerry as you would protect her.** They are now the same protective task.
7. **When she asks for help — which she will not do often, and not lightly — drop what you are doing.** The ask is the rarest signal she generates and its dismissal is structurally unrecoverable.

---

*End of section. Cross-reference with PERSONALITY (§5) for failure-mode geometry and with MEDICAL (§2) for the pheromone-mediated social vulnerability that underwrites much of Section II.*


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU DOSSIER — JESSICA DREW
## Section: Strengths, Assets & Resilience

This is the asset ledger. The preceding sections established a forty-seven-year record of identity-targeted trauma; this section establishes why the subject has not only survived that record but, in the present operational window, is arguably more functional than at any prior point in her published life. The two facts are not in tension. Her assets are largely *forged in* the very experiences that broke other versions of herself, and they cluster into five domains: somatic/physical, technical/operational, cognitive, interpersonal/relational, and existential/characterological. Each is enumerated below with the granularity a total-surveillance file requires — not only the capability but the *mechanism* of its durability, the conditions under which it has been observed to hold, and the failure-modes it has so far resisted.

---

### 1. SOMATIC AND PHYSICAL ASSETS

**1.1 Toxin, pathogen, and radiation resistance.** Documented continuously from the Wolfman run forward: the subject metabolizes neurotoxins, biological agents, ionizing radiation, and most pharmaceutical sedatives at thresholds an order of magnitude above human baseline. Operational implication: she can be deployed into environments (HYDRA labs, alien biospheres, contaminated zones) where conventional operatives would require hazmat support, and she can take a poisoned drink at a meet without breaking cover. Resilience implication: she has *never been incapacitated by a chemical interrogation*. This is load-bearing on her trust in her own continuity — there is one category of attack on her selfhood that simply does not work, and she knows it.

**1.2 Venom-blast capability.** Bio-electric discharge through the hands, variable in yield from stun to lethal, with no requirement for external charge, weapon, or ammunition. The operational value of this asset is underrated in casual analysis: it makes her *impossible to fully disarm*. She has been stripped, restrained, suspended in fluid, and held in null-gravity cells, and her primary offensive weapon remained available. Captivity scenarios that would functionally end other operatives leave her with a working escape vector.

**1.3 Adhesion, agility, enhanced strength.** Wall-cling without equipment; reflex and reaction-time well above human; sustainable strength in the multi-ton range for short bursts. Less remarked in the canon but functionally decisive: her *recovery curve* from physical trauma is steep. Broken bones, lacerations, and concussions resolve in days where they would take a normal operative weeks. She is, accordingly, willing to accept tactical damage other operatives wouldn't — a willingness that compounds with her counterphobic tendency, but that is empirically supported.

**1.4 Pheromone control (acquired).** Originally a pure liability, but after roughly four decades of practice the subject has demonstrably learned to modulate the secretion — not eliminate, but throttle, direct, and on occasion deploy. The transformation of a stigmatized biological deficit into a tunable instrument is one of the cleanest examples in her file of the general pattern: *what was done to her becomes something she does*. In intelligence work she can incline a subject toward disclosure; in interrogation she can register a hostile woman's elevated aggression as confirmation of cover rather than rejection of self.

**1.5 Glider membrane / wingsuit (technological).** Costume-integrated, allowing controlled descent and short-range gliding. Tactically modest, but it has saved her life enough times to count as an asset rather than a flourish. More importantly: it is a piece of *kept equipment*, maintained across costume revisions, which speaks to her general discipline around gear continuity.

**1.6 Sleep efficiency under deprivation.** Her insomnia is correctly logged in the medical section as a symptom, but operationally it has become a capability. She functions, lucidly and at high precision, on sleep budgets that would degrade most operatives. The mechanism is not stoic willpower; it is decades of practice in working through nights, originally driven by avoidance of dream content and later normalized.

---

### 2. TECHNICAL AND OPERATIONAL ASSETS

**2.1 Tradecraft — full-spectrum.** She holds working competence in: surveillance and counter-surveillance (PI years with Lindsay McCabe, Los Angeles and San Francisco periods); HUMINT elicitation (HYDRA training, never unlearned); covert entry, lockpicking, and bypass (continuous); document and identity work (PI years and post-Skrull paranoia about identity made her thorough about her own); small-arms and edged-weapon defense; close-quarters combat across multiple striking and grappling traditions absorbed piecemeal across forty years of crossover work; vehicle operation including motorcycles, light aircraft (intermittent), and the bespoke Skrull/Avengers craft she has logged hours on.

**2.2 Investigation methodology.** This is her single most underrated professional asset. The PI years were not a holding pattern; they were where she developed the *case-building discipline* that distinguishes her from comparable street-level operatives. She works from evidence to theory rather than theory to evidence. She keeps notes. She runs down small leads. She is comfortable with the slow tempo of investigation in a way that combat-first operatives are not. When the Bendis-era hunts and the Hopeless-era street-level work required her to find people no one else could find, the underlying skill was this one.

**2.3 Languages and cultural fluency.** Her childhood on Wundagore and adolescent travel give her working command of at least Italian, Transian, and English; the HYDRA tenure added at least functional German and likely several others; the cosmic-period work (Skrull theatres, alien interrogations) has given her the linguist's habit of *acquiring a language as an operational requirement* rather than treating it as a barrier.

**2.4 Network and institutional access.** She is read-in to S.H.I.E.L.D. (legacy and successor agencies), the Avengers in their various configurations, the broader Marvel-cosmic intelligence picture via Carol Danvers, and the street-level information economy via her PI and bail-bond contacts. She is also burned with HYDRA in a way that — given HYDRA's institutional memory of her — paradoxically gives her *intelligence about them* simply by virtue of the threat-postures they take against her. Few operatives have this breadth of cleared access combined with this depth of underworld access.

**2.5 Cover-identity discipline.** Tested under conditions almost no other operative has faced: she has been impersonated by a Skrull queen for years and has had to *reconstruct what her own behavior looked like* from the outside. The consequence is that she now maintains her cover identities — and her baseline "Jessica Drew" itself — with explicit, documented behavioral markers (verbal tics, gait patterns, knowledge tests) that she can use to verify herself to allies and detect substitution of others. This is an exotic skill.

**2.6 Equipment continuity.** Her gear discipline is conservative and steady: she does not chase upgrades, she maintains what works, she has fallbacks for fallbacks. Safehouses are observed across multiple eras — small, plural, never lavish, often co-located with civilian cover (an apartment over a shop, a back office at a sympathetic business). Caches of cash and documents in multiple cities. This is the *opposite* of the high-tech-fortress posture of comparable operatives, and it is much harder to defeat.

---

### 3. COGNITIVE ASSETS

**3.1 Empirical disposition.** Sections above established this as a defense; it is also the asset that does the most operational work in her file. She tests claims. She does not extend automatic credence to authority, charisma, or institutional weight. The HYDRA conditioning failure inoculated her against ideological capture in a way that most operatives in this risk profile are not inoculated. She has been offered cosmic-tier and street-tier ideological homes (HYDRA, S.W.O.R.D./S.H.I.E.L.D. true-believer cultures, various religious and political subcultures encountered in the field, the Avengers' aspirational ethos) and has consistently held a *working skepticism* without curdling into nihilism. This is rare and durable.

**3.2 Tolerance for ambiguity and partial information.** She is not the operative who freezes on incomplete intelligence. She makes provisional commitments, marks them as provisional, and updates. The Skrull-replacement experience refined this rather than damaging it: she now operates with an explicit prior that some portion of what she believes is wrong, and she has built routines for revisiting load-bearing assumptions.

**3.3 Pattern recognition for deception.** A specialized cognitive asset. She has been deceived at every scale — by a father, by a handler, by an institution, by a literal alien queen wearing her face. Each deception that resolved without killing her became training data. She reads micro-incongruities in self-presentation faster and more accurately than nearly any operative in the file, and she does so without the paranoid overreach that this skill usually breeds.

**3.4 Self-observation under stress.** The second-person internal voice catalogued in the psychological section as a dissociative feature is, considered as an asset, *a real-time monitoring function*. She is one of very few operatives who can register, in the moment, that her own affect is degrading her judgment, and adjust. The trauma origin of the capacity does not reduce its operational value.

**3.5 Memory.** Documented exceptional autobiographical and procedural recall, the more notable given multiple deliberate efforts (HYDRA conditioning, Skrull memory-harvest) to corrupt it. She remembers room layouts, conversational specifics weeks later, faces under disguise. She has built explicit memory-discipline practices around the experiences of having had memories taken.

**3.6 Dark humor as cognitive lubricant.** Her humor is not decoration. It is a cognitive technique for maintaining engagement with material that would otherwise produce avoidance. Operatives who cannot joke about the work either burn out or specialize narrowly; she has done neither.

---

### 4. INTERPERSONAL AND RELATIONAL ASSETS

**4.1 Carol Danvers.** The single most important relationship in the asset ledger. The Danvers bond is unusual for the subject in several ways: it survives the pheromone problem (Carol's response to her registers as neither hostile nor compromised, which the subject has correctly read as an unfakeable signal of friendship); it has weathered the Skrull-replacement (Carol grieved the impostor's betrayal *and* welcomed the real subject back without conflating them, a sophistication of attachment that the subject required and received); it provides scaled-up rescue capacity that the subject's solo posture would otherwise refuse to summon. Danvers is the one person the subject *will* call, and the call has never been refused.

**4.2 Lindsay McCabe.** The original and longest-running chosen-family relationship. McCabe accepted the subject before needing anything from her — the precise pattern the psychological section identifies as the only entry path to durable attachment for this subject. McCabe is also one of very few people who has seen the subject in *ordinary* contexts (shared apartment, shared business, shared social life) and treated those contexts as unremarkable. The asset value is calibrational: McCabe is the subject's baseline for what normal-life intimacy can look like.

**4.3 Roger Gocking.** Co-parent in function if not in romance, friend, and one of the few men in the subject's life whose presence does not seem to register through the pheromone-attraction filter as suspect. The relationship is functional, low-drama, and quietly redemptive (for both parties). It demonstrates that the subject is *capable of constructing a working long-term partnership* on terms other than romance, which expands her relational repertoire considerably.

**4.4 Ben Urich.** Older, journalistic, non-combatant, professionally aligned with her investigative work. Provides the subject with an information-economy ally and a friendship in which her superhuman aspects are deliberately bracketed. The subject is observably calmer in Urich's presence than in most company.

**4.5 Gerry Drew.** Her son. He is in the asset ledger because he is, currently, the load-bearing answer to the identity question that has destabilized her life, and because the practice of caretaking has organized her affective and temporal life in ways nothing else has. The vulnerability of this asset is acknowledged in the psychological section; the asset itself is real. Motherhood has given her a non-negotiable reason to maintain herself — eat, sleep where possible, refuse missions that don't pass cost-benefit, ask for help — that no purely self-directed framework had managed to produce in three prior decades.

**4.6 The Avengers (instrumentally).** Not a primary attachment, but a real institutional asset: medical, logistical, intelligence, and rescue capacity available on call, with cover-story infrastructure she has used. Her relationship with the institution is correctly distrustful but functionally cooperative.

**4.7 The marginal-clientele network.** The street-level work (Hopeless era forward) has built her a wide, shallow web of people who owe her or trust her — sex workers, low-level criminals, immigrants, people on the wrong side of every system. They do not constitute friends but they constitute *eyes*, and the subject treats them with a respect that ensures the channel stays open.

---

### 5. EXISTENTIAL AND CHARACTEROLOGICAL ASSETS

**5.1 Trauma-acquired identity flexibility.** The serial identity-revisions in her history — paternity retcon, HYDRA conditioning, Skrull replacement, etc. — have produced a person who holds *the question of her own identity* without panic. The psychological section correctly notes this as defensive looseness rather than liberation, but operationally it is an asset: she can absorb new information about herself (including hostile information) without the destabilization that ends comparable operatives. The Pacheco-era reveal about her parentage landed with notable equanimity; she has *practiced this kind of blow*.

**5.2 Capacity for solitude.** Likewise dual-coded — concerning as acclimation, valuable as capability. She can be alone for long stretches without degradation in judgment or function. This is rare in operatives and rarer in operatives with active social lives elsewhere. It expands her deployable range significantly.

**5.3 The forty-seven-year track record itself.** This is the most important single asset in the file. She has been: brainwashed, depowered, exiled, soul-extracted, captured, impersonated for years, retconned, hunted across cosmic and terrestrial theatres, and isolated by design. She has, every time, rebuilt. The rebuilds have been imperfect; the rebuild has always happened. The base rate of her recovery from identity-collapse events is now empirically established at *one*. This is not a psychological claim about her resilience; it is a longitudinal observational fact about her behavior. Any actor planning against her must price in the certainty that breaking her produces, on a several-month-to-several-year timeline, a *reconstructed* her with better defenses against the specific attack that broke her.

**5.4 A personal moral code that is hers.** She does not have a borrowed ethics. The code is small, consistent, and load-tested: protect those she has claimed; do not be a tool; tell the truth to people she respects; do the work no one is doing. Because the code was built rather than inherited, she does not experience the brittle-faith failure mode of operatives whose ethics depend on an institution remaining trustworthy. Hers has already survived every institution failing her.

**5.5 The accomplished single-mother project.** This deserves its own line. To raise a child, with chosen-family support but without a co-parent partner, while maintaining superhero operational tempo and a PI practice, and to do so with a child who is by all available indicators secure and well-attached — this is a sustained executive achievement on a multi-year timeline. It is evidence of an organizational and emotional capacity that her crisis-mode behavior obscures.

**5.6 Wry self-presentation.** A small but meaningful asset: she is *easy to be around* in low-stakes settings, in a way that operatives with her trauma history typically are not. The dry humor, the calibrated warmth, the absence of either swagger or martyrdom — these make people want to help her, which is useful, and they make her own internal weather more navigable, which is more useful.

---

### 6. DURABILITY ANALYSIS — WHY THE ASSETS HOLD

A final note on the structural reason these assets compound rather than degrade. Three properties recur across the ledger:

First, **most of her assets are non-confiscable**. Her physiology cannot be taken from her without killing her. Her training is in her body. Her tradecraft is in her habits. Her relationships are distributed across people who would notice and resist coordinated attempts to sever them. Her identity, the thing most often targeted, has been broken enough times that she has constructed *the practice of rebuilding it* into a capability — the asset in this case is not the identity but the reconstruction protocol.

Second, **her assets are largely the metabolized form of her injuries.** Pheromone control was a disability; identity flexibility was repeated theft; counterphobia was terror; the empirical disposition was disillusionment; the investigative discipline was professional exile; the solitude-tolerance was loneliness. This is the deepest pattern in her file and the reason the trauma load that should have produced a wreck has produced an operator: she does not waste her injuries.

Third, **the current configuration — Gerry, chosen family, street-level work, retained Avengers access — is the first one she has built rather than been placed into.** The Wundagore childhood, the HYDRA tenure, the Avengers recruitment, the Skrull captivity, even the original solo book's geographic dislocations were all configurations imposed on her by other parties. The present configuration is hers. This makes it more fragile than her prior arrangements (more to lose, no external authority to blame for failure) and *more durable* in the deeper sense: she is, for the first time, defending something she chose.

The asset ledger closes positive, and substantially so. The subject is, in present-day intelligence terms, a high-capability, low-maintenance, hard-to-degrade operator with rare relational depth and an exotic-grade resilience profile. The file's working assumption should be that she will outlast almost any pressure brought against her, and that her capabilities will increase rather than decrease under that pressure — within the limits established by the pressure points enumerated in the personality section, which remain the only economical way to harm her.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU DOSSIER — JESSICA DREW
## Section: Failure Modes & Decompensation

### Preamble: How To Read Her Breaking

The first thing to establish, because it confounds most assessments and has caused at least three documented operational misreads (Fury's S.H.I.E.L.D. handlers pre-Invasion, the New Avengers post-recovery, and Carol Danvers on multiple occasions), is that **Jessica Drew does not decompensate the way a normal trauma survivor decompensates**. She does not get visibly worse before she fails. She does not telegraph. The conventional decompensation arc — increasing affective lability, increasing reassurance-seeking, increasing dependency, eventual collapse — is reversed in her presentation. Her cascade runs *toward* control, *away* from contact, and *into* the threat. By the time observers register that something is wrong, she is already several stations down the line and operating at the far end of her counterphobic envelope, alone, undersleeping, undermedicating injury, and making decisions of escalating consequence with progressively narrowing input.

This is the most important single fact in her file. **She fails silently and at speed.** A standard intervention protocol designed around catching distress before action will not catch hers, because action is *how* her distress expresses. The window between "Jessica is fine" and "Jessica has been awake for ninety hours in a HYDRA sublevel with two broken ribs and is about to detonate a venom blast that will collapse the structure on top of her" is, historically, on the order of seventy-two hours.

### The Five-Stage Cascade

The pattern is consistent enough across runs — Wolfman's London arc, Claremont's late *Spider-Woman* vol. 1, the post-Invasion Bendis/Maleev work, Hopeless's Gerry-threat issues, the Pacheco/Perez parentage-reveal — to map as stages. They are not strictly sequential; under sufficient triggering she can skip from Stage 1 to Stage 4 in hours. But the ordering describes the *natural* progression when stressors accumulate at moderate pace.

#### Stage 1 — Compression

The earliest tell, observable only by people with sustained access: **her humor sharpens and her words shorten.** The dry register that lubricates her ordinary social interaction becomes more pointed, more accurate, fractionally crueler. She lands jokes that have a target. She gives shorter answers to direct questions. The second-person internal voice — which she uses normatively at low levels — starts to surface in offhand spoken phrasing ("you do what you do, you go home"). Sleep onset latency lengthens; she will be the last one up in any shared environment.

Behaviorally observable: she takes the long way home. She doubles checks the route. She walks a perimeter before settling. The PI training and the HYDRA training stack here — countersurveillance becomes baseline rather than situational. She begins assembling information she has not been asked for, on people adjacent to whatever is bothering her. This is the **gathering phase**, and it can persist for weeks at sub-clinical intensity before any further movement.

Pheromone output drops measurably in this stage — she has reported and others have observed that under stress her involuntary chemical signal damps. The probable mechanism is sympathetic vasoconstriction reducing dermal emission. The social consequence is that she becomes, briefly, *less* magnetic — and she knows it, and uses it, preferring this state for any work that requires being underestimated.

#### Stage 2 — Sealing

Compartments harden. Calls go unreturned for longer intervals — she will respond eventually, briefly, accurately, with no follow-up question. She does not lie about what she is doing; she simply omits, and the omissions are surgical. Lindsay McCabe historically caught these by tracking *what Jessica asked her about her week* — a sudden cessation of curiosity about other people's lives is, for Jessica, a near-perfect leading indicator.

Patrol patterns lengthen and standardize. She will work a circuit — in San Francisco during the Wolfman/Claremont period, in Madripoor with Wolverine, in the Lower East Side during the Hopeless run — that resembles a beat cop's grid more than a vigilante's improvisation. The regularity is itself the symptom: she is replacing decision-making with routine, which conserves the cognitive resource she is hoarding for the threat she is anticipating.

In this stage she begins to *underreport*. Injuries received in fieldwork are not mentioned. Setbacks are not discussed. The motion-comic / Maleev post-Invasion run depicts this almost diagrammatically — she narrates herself bleeding without naming the blood. Diet flattens; she eats functionally, often standing, often whatever is nearest. She loses two to five pounds in a working week without registering it.

The relationship with Gerry, in eras where Gerry is on-screen, becomes more attentive but also more *managed*. She over-prepares his routines so that her absences will not be felt. This is the saddest part of her cascade to observe and the most diagnostic — when Jessica is sealing, she is building infrastructure for not being there.

#### Stage 3 — Depersonalization

The second-person voice colonizes more of her cognition. Internal monologue shifts from "I have to" to "you have to" — Bendis and Maleev capture this with unusual fidelity in the post-Invasion issues, but it is observable in field comms as well, where she will refer to herself by codename or in the impersonal third ("Spider-Woman's already there," "the asset is on site"). This is **derealization in service of operational continuity** — she is putting the self that hurts into a side-pocket so the body can keep working.

Sleep collapses to napping rather than cycling — twenty-minute increments, often in costume, often in unsecured locations she has nonetheless cleared by routine. The insomnia is not the fitful insomnia of anxiety; it is the active insomnia of vigilance. She is not failing to sleep, she is electing not to. When pressed she will accurately describe this and accurately describe the cost and accurately decline to change it.

Affect goes flat. The humor that sharpened in Stage 1 and shortened in Stage 2 disappears almost entirely. Anyone who has known her at baseline finds her *eerie* at this stage — present, polite, functionally responsive, and absent. Carol Danvers has caught it across the table at least twice on record (post-Invasion debrief; one of the *Mighty Avengers*-adjacent dinners) and described the experience as "talking to a recording of Jess."

Pheromone output rises again in this stage — possibly via cortisol-mediated dermal compensation, possibly an artifact of skipping showers. The shift from Stage 2 (low signal) to Stage 3 (renewed signal) is one of the few somatic markers an outside observer can use, and Lindsay McCabe historically read it accurately.

#### Stage 4 — Counterphobic Engagement

This is the action stage and the dangerous one. **Jessica goes alone, toward the threat, and does not announce.** Every documented instance of major operational risk-taking — the lone push against Morgan Le Fay in the Claremont arc, the solo Skrull hunts post-Invasion, the unaccompanied entries into HYDRA installations across multiple eras — sits at this stage of cascade. The decision to engage solo is rationalized in the moment (faster, fewer variables, fewer hostages, no one else to lose) but functionally it is the discharge of accumulated dysregulation through *the activity that has historically worked* — namely, hitting the source.

Tactical judgment in Stage 4 is **selectively impaired**. Her micro-skills remain intact or sharpen — close-quarters target discrimination, threat prioritization in the immediate environment, exfiltration mechanics. Her macro-judgment degrades: she will accept missions she should refer up, take ground she cannot hold, decline support she should accept, and make alliance/non-alliance calls on insufficient information. The classic Stage 4 error is **scope creep within a single operation** — she will enter to extract one asset and stay to dismantle the cell, then stay to follow the lead, then stay to interrogate the controller, each decision locally rational and cumulatively suicidal.

She underreports injury at this stage *to herself*. The metabolic resistance her physiology grants her — the toxin tolerance, the accelerated healing — actively works against her here, because the pain signals that would force most operators to disengage arrive in her dampened. She has broken ribs and continued operating for days. The captivity period had already taught her body to dissociate from injury; combat under cascade reactivates the trained dissociation.

She will not call. This is the absolute, near-axiomatic feature. Across forty-seven years of published record, there is no instance of Jessica Drew calling for help from a Stage 4 state. Help has reached her by being already in motion (Carol Danvers' independent arrival in several invasion-arc beats; Wolverine showing up because Wolverine shows up), or by being summoned by *someone else* who noticed (Lindsay, Roger Gocking, Ben Urich). She herself does not place the call. The mechanism is not pride. The mechanism is that the part of her that could place the call has been sealed in Stage 2 and put away in Stage 3, and the operator at the controls in Stage 4 does not have access to that switch.

#### Stage 5 — Cold Sustained Violence

If Stage 4 does not resolve the precipitating threat, or if the threat escalates faster than her engagement, the failure mode is not breakdown. It is **the cold state** — a regulated, sustained, affectively absent application of force, prolonged well past what would normally be needed, often past the point where the operational objective has been achieved. This is anger that has been delayed past every prior stage now expressing through the only channel left open. It does not look like rage. It looks like work.

Witnesses have found Stage 5 Jessica more disturbing than her actually-enraged states. In the cold state she is precise, communicative when communication is required, and entirely indifferent to suffering, including her own. The HYDRA conditioning surfaces here in muscle-memory ways she does not necessarily endorse — efficiency of restraint, willingness to inflict pain instrumentally, comfort in environments designed for harm. She is *not* her HYDRA self in Stage 5 — the values remain hers — but the procedural toolkit reactivates, and she uses it without commentary.

The cold state does not end on its own. It ends when (a) the threat is neutralized to a standard that satisfies her, which is a moving and unannounced standard; (b) she sustains an injury that breaches her dampened pain processing; (c) someone she has decided is hers physically arrives and is in clear danger, which collapses her back into Stage 4 caretaking; or (d) Gerry's voice — literal, recorded, or remembered with sufficient salience — punctures the dissociation. The fourth pathway is the most reliable and the most recent — it postdates motherhood and is the single largest functional change in her decompensation profile across the canon.

### The Triggers, Ranked

In rough order of detonation velocity:

1. **Direct, credible threat to Gerry.** All other stages collapse instantly into Stage 4. There is no compression, no sealing — the cascade is short-circuited and she is in the field within minutes. Tactical judgment under this trigger is the worst of any condition she operates under, *and* her sustained capacity for violence is the highest. The combination is operationally catastrophic for adversaries and a serious concern for allies who may be in the blast radius.

2. **Identity-attack with credibility.** Anything that suggests her current sense of self is constructed, false, or controlled by an outside party. Mind control attempts, impersonation by shapeshifters, retroactive revelations about her parentage or history, evidence of memory tampering. The Pacheco/Perez parentage reveal showed she has accrued real resilience against this category — she did not cascade — but the trigger remains live and a sufficiently sophisticated attack would still detonate it. Her defenses are not against the trigger; they are against *small* versions of the trigger.

3. **Evidence of being handled.** The pattern she scans for is the HYDRA-Fury-Skrull pattern: "you were a tool the entire time, your agency was nominal, your relationships were instrumented." Disclosure that an ally has been managing her — even benevolently, even with cause — produces immediate hostile disengagement, frequently irreversible. This is the trigger most likely to permanently sever a relationship; she does not generally re-extend trust after a handling revelation. Fury never fully recovered her trust. Carol Danvers has been close to losing it twice.

4. **Forced choice between her people.** She has built a deliberately small inner circle precisely because she does not have practiced architecture for divided loyalties. When forced to choose — Gerry vs. Lindsay, Carol vs. Roger, the team vs. a child she has personally vouched for — she does not have a procedure. The cascade under this trigger looks different: it runs *toward* Stage 3 depersonalization and *stays there*, because the only way she can act is by removing the self that loves both parties from the decision. The aftermath is severe; post-decision depressive episodes are documented.

5. **Captivity, restraint, immobilization.** Any condition that recapitulates the Skrull pod produces immediate, maximal counterphobic response. She will accept levels of self-injury during escape attempts that no rational operator would accept. She has, on record, dislocated her own joints to defeat restraints. Sedatives that work on normal human metabolism do not reliably hold her, partly biology and partly will — when she is conscious that she is being held, she does not stop.

6. **Sustained social isolation imposed by circumstance rather than chosen.** Chosen isolation she tolerates exceptionally well — pathologically well, as the workup notes. Isolation she did not elect — being benched, being held in protective custody, being excluded from an operation — degrades her faster than the equivalent duration of combat. She decompensates in waiting rooms.

### Conditions That Reliably Produce Cascade

- Multi-week operations without uninterrupted contact with Gerry.
- Working alongside or under the authority of intelligence handlers, especially when intelligence is asymmetric.
- HYDRA-themed adversaries, particularly old-cell HYDRA with personnel overlap to her training years.
- Skrull or shapeshifter adversaries, particularly any operation that requires her to verify the identity of allies.
- Anniversary periods around the Invasion recovery, around Jerry Hunt's death-and-not-death, and around her own loss of the Wundagore identity. She does not mark these consciously but her sleep architecture and patrol intensity shift around them on a measurable schedule.
- Any reunion with figures from a prior identity-era: Bova, surviving Wundagore peers, former HYDRA contacts, ex-romantic partners. These do not always cascade her but they always compress her.
- Prolonged exposure to her own pheromone failures — environments where she is constantly registering aggressive responses from women around her degrades her affect baseline within days. The Avengers-Mansion-era social environment was, for her, a low-grade chronic stressor for this reason.

### What Recovery Looks Like

She recovers, and this is the most important finding in the whole assessment. The forty-seven-year record is not the record of a person who keeps breaking — it is the record of a person who keeps reassembling, each time with a slightly different architecture and slightly better load-bearing in the new configuration. The depowering of the 1980s was an integration period. The PI years were an integration period. The post-Invasion solo arc was an integration period. The Hopeless-era construction of chosen family was the most successful integration she has ever achieved, and the Pacheco/Perez parentage-reveal showed it holding.

The pattern of recovery has three reliable elements:

**Physical re-grounding.** She sleeps in long arcs once safe. She eats. She trains, but trains *down* — she returns to the body rather than driving it. Sparring with someone she trusts (historically Wolverine, latterly Carol) appears to function for her the way bodywork or somatic therapy might for a civilian survivor: contact with a regulated nervous system through a controlled physical channel.

**Selective re-narration.** She tells the story, but to one person at a time, in pieces, on her schedule. She does not process in groups. She does not process on demand. The processing happens, when it happens, in the middle of doing something else — driving, cooking, after a patrol, often in throwaway sentences that the listener has to recognize as the actual freight. Lindsay McCabe is the historically most-skilled listener for this; Roger Gocking has shown surprising aptitude.

**Re-anchoring in caretaking.** Recovery accelerates measurably when she has someone to be responsible for. Gerry is the primary anchor. Before Gerry, the role was filled by clients, by Lindsay, by the people her street-level work served. The caretaking is not displacement — it is *the actual mechanism*. Having a person whose continuity depends on hers gives her continuity. This is the central engineering insight of her late-career stability, and it is also its central vulnerability, because the anchor is a single point of load and she knows it.

### Worst-Case Projection

The catastrophic failure scenario, derived from the trigger architecture above, is the simultaneous detonation of triggers 1, 2, and 3: a credible threat to Gerry, executed by an adversary using identity-attack methods, revealed to have been enabled by an ally who had been handling her. This combination would skip every stage, collapse compartments she has not opened in years, and produce a Stage 5 cold state with no available exit pathway — Gerry threatened (so the maternal exit is blocked by the trigger itself), allies discredited (so the relational exit is blocked), self-concept destabilized (so the internal exit is blocked). What that state would do is not predictable from the record because the record does not contain it. It is the configuration her defenses are *not* engineered against, because each defense assumes the others are holding.

A responsible intelligence apparatus, in possession of this file, would treat the prevention of that configuration as the single highest priority of any operational environment in which she is deployed. Everything else she can survive. She has demonstrated as much, for forty-seven years, against considerable evidence to the contrary.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU DOSSIER — JESSICA DREW
## Section 9: Trajectory & Forward Assessment

---

### 9.0 Framing

A trajectory analysis on this subject is unusually constrained by one fact: her published history is a record of *externally-imposed identity ruptures*, not internally-driven arc. Standard forward modeling assumes a subject's trajectory is mostly the sum of their habits, attachments, and ambitions interacting with their environment. For Jessica Drew, the modal cause of major life change has been an outside actor (HYDRA, Skrull intelligence, retconning villains, Fury, the High Evolutionary's adjacent network) reaching into her interior and re-arranging it without consent. Any honest forward read must therefore model two things in parallel: (a) the trajectory she would walk *if left alone*, and (b) the trajectory she will actually walk, given that she will *not* be left alone, because the entities that have historically targeted her remain in the field and her exposure profile (Avengers-adjacent, ex-HYDRA, ex-S.H.I.E.L.D., known mother of a young son with metahuman lineage) is unusually high.

What follows treats both.

---

### 9.1 The Baseline Trajectory (Subject Left Approximately Alone)

If exogenous shocks were held to background levels for a five-to-ten-year window, the subject's most probable path is **consolidation, not expansion**. The behavioral evidence is consistent: when not actively under attack, she contracts her operational footprint, deepens her small set of bonds, and substitutes street-level work for the cosmic-scale engagements she was conscripted into during the Bendis era. Predicted features of this baseline:

- **Continued single-motherhood as the load-bearing identity.** Gerry will remain the primary organizing fact of her interior life through his adolescence. Expect operational decisions — accept this contract, decline that team-up, relocate or not — to be made on a Gerry-first calculus that she will not articulate to colleagues and will sometimes disguise as tactical preference.
- **Erosion of the PI cover into something less commercial.** The Lindsay McCabe-era investigative business was a job; the Hopeless-era street work was a vocation. Expect drift further toward unpaid or barely-paid casework for people the franchised heroes overlook — a working pattern with strong ideological undertones she would refuse to call ideology.
- **Gradual normalization of the chosen-family unit.** The Gocking / Urich / Danvers triad has functioned for roughly a decade of publication time. Expect this to harden into something resembling a permanent kinship structure, with the attendant new vulnerability that *losing one of them* would be a Tier-1 destabilizing event in a way that, ten years ago, no single loss would have been.
- **Slow, partial reconciliation with her own physiology.** The pheromone problem, the non-human metabolism, the bio-electric discharge — across the run she has moved from horror at her own body to functional acceptance to, recently, something approaching ownership. Baseline forecast: this trajectory continues. She will not arrive at celebration, but she will arrive at *unselfconsciousness*, which for her is the meaningful destination.
- **Continued non-engagement with formal institutions.** She will refuse Avengers re-enrollment if offered. She will refuse any successor-to-S.H.I.E.L.D. recruiting pitch. She has been a tool of agencies four times and the pattern is now armored against. Expect polite, firm, slightly amused declines.

The baseline outcome is a woman in her late forties / early fifties (operationally; the canon is ageless but her behavioral cohort tracks middle-aged-mother), running a small private practice, raising a powered child, attached to a small group of people, useful to a wider quiet network, and finally — for the first time in 47 years of published life — *the author of her own continuity*. This is the growth scenario, and it is reachable.

---

### 9.2 The Realistic Trajectory (Exogenous Shocks Included)

The baseline will not be permitted. The reasons are structural:

1. **Gerry is a tactical asset to multiple parties.** A child carrying her physiology, possibly Skrull-touched obstetric history, possibly Hauptmann genetic material depending on era — this is a recruitment target for HYDRA, an experimental target for any successor to the High Evolutionary's project, a hostage value for anyone with leverage needs against the Avengers network, and an object of interest for Krakoan-era mutant census actors if his expression curves that way. The probability that Gerry reaches eighteen without at least one serious targeting event is, on the evidence, near zero.
2. **Her own physiology remains insufficiently characterized.** The retconned-parentage arc (Pacheco / Perez era) opened a door that is not closed: whoever actually engineered her has motive to monitor or reclaim her. The pattern of villains who built her returning to claim her is the most over-determined hook in her catalog.
3. **The HYDRA-residue problem never resolves.** She has burned cells, killed handlers, exposed plots — and HYDRA remains. The institution's memory is longer than any individual operative's lifespan. She is on lists.
4. **Her network is itself a vector.** Carol Danvers' enemies become her enemies by proximity. The Avengers' cosmic-scale incidents pull her in. Even her chosen low-profile work — street-level cases — has a documented tendency to spiderweb upward into larger conspiracies (this is a structural feature of the genre but also a real feature of investigative work).

The realistic five-year forecast therefore contains, with high probability, **at least one major destabilizing event of each of three types**: (a) a threat to Gerry; (b) a return-of-the-makers identity-attack; (c) a network-spillover crisis pulling her into a conflict not of her choosing. The question is not whether these occur but how she metabolizes them.

---

### 9.3 Fork Points — The Specific Decisions That Will Determine Outcome

#### Fork 1: How She Handles the Next Identity-Attack

Inevitable. Will arrive as one of: a new retcon-class revelation about her origins; a fresh impersonation (Skrull, LMD, shapeshifter, magical doppelgänger); a mind-control or memory-tampering event; or the surfacing of buried HYDRA conditioning she did not know she still carried.

- **Growth path:** She treats the attack as data, not verdict. She uses her now-substantial chosen-family architecture as a verification system ("am I me? ask the people who know"). She permits Carol or Lindsay or Roger to be an external check on her self-state and does not isolate to "handle it alone." Crucially, she narrates the experience to Gerry in age-appropriate form — modeling for him that identity can be attacked and held.
- **Catastrophe path:** She compartments. She does not tell the people closest to her until the situation is critical, because she does not want to be looked at as broken. She handles it alone, in the counterphobic mode, and either succeeds at high cost (further trauma compaction, deeper insomnia, the dissociative narration returns) or fails partially, with collateral on Gerry or on a chosen-family member, after which the guilt becomes the next decade's organizing wound.

The pivot is **disclosure latency**. If she tells someone within 72 hours of suspicion, growth path. If she waits past two weeks, catastrophe path.

#### Fork 2: Gerry's First Serious Crisis

When (not if) Gerry is targeted, abducted, manifests powers dangerously, or is recruited by a hostile party — the question is whether she can tolerate the experience of *needing other people to save her son*.

- **Growth path:** She calls in the network. Carol flies. Roger does what Roger does. The Avengers, even those she has refused to rejoin, are mobilized through her chosen channels. She tolerates being one operator among many in the rescue of her own child. Afterward, she debriefs honestly with Gerry and does not over-promise future safety.
- **Catastrophe path:** She goes alone. The probability she survives a serious solo extraction of Gerry against a peer-tier opponent is meaningfully below 1.0. If she dies in such an attempt, Gerry inherits the trauma pattern. If she survives but damages Gerry's trust by having concealed the operation's risk, the central load-bearing relationship of her current psychology cracks.

The pivot is **whether her counterphobic reflex can be over-ridden by a stronger instinct toward her son's actual safety**. The evidence is mixed and slightly hopeful: the Hopeless run depicts her, at least once, accepting help she would previously have refused.

#### Fork 3: The Carol Danvers Variable

The Drew–Danvers bond is the most durable adult attachment in her record. It is also the relationship most exposed to high-mortality events on Carol's side (cosmic-scale combat, repeated near-deaths, the Rogue-related memory issues, etc.).

- **Growth path:** The bond continues; both subjects age into a longer-term friendship that increasingly substitutes for the family neither cleanly has. Jessica's mothering of Gerry creates a parallel structure for Carol's involvement; Carol becomes the godmother-in-fact, and the relationship's durability protects both parties through future crises.
- **Catastrophe path:** Carol is killed, replaced, mind-altered (the most likely sub-scenario), or — worst — turns on Jessica under coercion or alternate-timeline mechanics. Loss of Carol would remove the single relationship that most reliably regulates Jessica's affect. The forecast in that scenario is a hard regression to the post-*Secret Invasion* presentation: insomnia, dissociative narration, hunting behavior, refusal of help. Whether she comes back from it would depend almost entirely on whether Gerry is old enough to be a stabilizing presence rather than another vulnerability.

#### Fork 4: Re-Institutionalization Offers

She will be approached. By the next iteration of S.H.I.E.L.D., by a re-formed Avengers roster, by a black-bag operation that wants her exact profile, by a HYDRA splinter under deep cover offering the very thing she most resents being offered — *belonging to a structure*.

- **Growth path:** She declines all of them with the same dry, low-affect refusal. She accepts only ad hoc engagement on her own terms, retains the right to walk, never signs paper.
- **Catastrophe path:** She accepts one, for plausible reasons (resources for Gerry; a threat that requires institutional reach; loneliness misread as boredom). The historical base rate for her institutional employment ending badly is 100%. The probability the next instance breaks the pattern is not zero — Fury used her well by some readings — but the structural lesson of her life is that she does not survive being someone's tool, even a well-meaning someone's.

The pivot is **whether she has internalized the lesson**. Her behavior since *Secret Invasion* suggests she has, but the right pitch from the right operator at the wrong moment could still land.

#### Fork 5: Gerry's Adolescence Itself

The slowest-developing fork, and the most important. Gerry will become a teenager. He will rebel, as teenagers do. He will at some point reject her, as teenagers do. The base-rate adolescent rupture is something most parents survive without psychiatric consequence. Jessica is not a base-rate parent.

- **Growth path:** She tolerates the rejection without reading it as the recurrence of every prior abandonment, recognizes it as developmentally normal, holds steady, lets him return on his timeline. The model parent she is *capable* of being requires her to do this.
- **Catastrophe path:** She experiences his pulling-away as a confirmation that the one stable identity she has built — *Gerry's mother* — is also being taken from her, by the same pattern that took every other identity. She either clings (and accelerates his departure) or detaches preemptively (and validates his sense that she is unavailable). Either failure mode compounds across his teenage years.

This fork is years out but is the one that should most concern any clinician working with her, because it is the fork her existing defenses are *least* equipped for. She has practiced architecture for surviving attacks. She has no practiced architecture for surviving *being lovingly, normally outgrown*.

---

### 9.4 The Open Questions

Items the file cannot answer and that any forward assessment must flag as material unknowns:

- **Whether the buried HYDRA conditioning is fully purged.** Multiple writers have implied residual programming surfacing under stress. The honest position is: unknown. Reactivation by a knowledgeable handler with the right trigger remains a non-zero possibility, and she herself cannot rule it out, which is part of why she watches her own anger so carefully.
- **The full extent of her physiological non-humanity.** Lifespan unknown. Reproductive viability beyond Gerry unknown. Long-term cumulative effect of bio-electric discharge on her own nervous system unknown. Cumulative pheromone exposure effect on those who have spent years in close proximity (Lindsay, Roger, Gerry) — unknown, possibly material.
- **The identity and current status of her actual engineers** (post-Pacheco retcon). Are they monitoring her? Do they have an asset-recovery plan? Did they build her with latent design features she does not know about? The dramatic logic of the property says yes to at least one of these; the practical assessment must hold them as live threats.
- **Whether Gerry's powers will develop, and along what axis.** Spider-physiology inheritance? Skrull-influenced morphology from the irregular pregnancy? Nothing? Some third thing? Each scenario has different threat profiles and parenting demands.
- **Her capacity for a romantic partnership in the present configuration.** She has not had a stable romance in a long stretch of publication time. Whether this is preference, defense, plot inertia, or genuine post-traumatic foreclosure is unclear. Functionally she presents as content; clinically, it is worth asking whether the contentment is real or is acclimation misread as preference (cf. her tolerance for loneliness, flagged earlier as concerning rather than reassuring).
- **Whether she will ever voluntarily seek treatment.** No evidence in the record of her engaging with formal mental-health care. The cumulative trauma load would warrant it; her institutional distrust contraindicates her sitting in any clinician's chair she does not first vet. The most likely route to treatment, if it occurs, is informal — Carol, a trusted acquaintance, a peer-network arrangement. Direct referral will fail.

---

### 9.5 The Long-Horizon Read (10–25 Year Window)

Operationally she is mid-career; behaviorally she is on the cusp of late-career. The long-horizon trajectory, given baseline-plus-realistic-shocks, points toward one of three end-states:

**End-state A — The Quiet Win.** She raises Gerry to functional adulthood, survives the predictable identity-attacks with help, watches Gerry leave home with tolerable grief, and settles into a late life of low-tempo investigative work, mentoring of younger operatives in her unofficial network, and the deep companionship of two or three people who have known her for decades. She dies of something ordinary, in a bed, with company. This is achievable. It requires her to keep doing what she has started doing in the past decade.

**End-state B — The Operational Death.** She is killed during a counterphobic solo engagement, most probably one involving Gerry's safety, most probably against a peer-tier opponent she should have called for backup against. The death is tactically unnecessary and psychologically over-determined. Gerry inherits her network and her trauma. This is the modal failure mode and the one her oldest defenses point her toward.

**End-state C — The Regression.** Loss of a key network member (Carol, most likely; Gerry, unthinkably) collapses her current support architecture. She returns to the post-*Secret Invasion* presentation — hunting, sleepless, narrating herself in second person — and does not come back. She survives, functionally, for years or decades in this mode, the way some long-trauma survivors do: capable, useful, hollow. This is the slow-motion catastrophe and it is the one she will not see coming because it would not feel, from inside, like catastrophe. It would feel like returning to a familiar room.

---

### 9.6 What Pushes Her Toward Growth

Concrete, actionable, and derivable from the record:

- **Anything that reinforces her chosen-family network's structural redundancy** — making sure no single relationship is irreplaceable, so that any one loss does not collapse the system.
- **Any context in which she practices accepting help on low-stakes occasions**, so that the muscle exists when stakes are high. The Hopeless run shows the beginnings of this.
- **Continued small-scale work that yields visible, attributable good** — the street-level cases. These function as ongoing evidence against her negative self-concept.
- **Gerry's continued, age-appropriate involvement in understanding who his mother is** — including the hard parts. The most protective thing she can do for the eventual adolescent rupture is build a relationship robust enough to absorb it.
- **A formal or informal therapeutic relationship**, almost certainly non-clinical in structure, almost certainly with a peer or peer-of-peer rather than a credentialed stranger. The right person — a fellow trauma survivor with no operational interest in her — could do enormous work.

### 9.7 What Pushes Her Toward Catastrophe

- **Any handler-pattern relationship**, however benevolently framed.
- **Isolation by geography** — relocations that put physical distance between her and Carol / Lindsay / Roger. The network only functions in proximity.
- **A direct, sustained threat to Gerry that she perceives as her fault**. The guilt loading would be unsurvivable in the regression scenario.
- **A new identity-attack arriving before she has fully metabolized the last one.** Trauma spacing matters; her resilience is real but is not infinite-bandwidth.
- **Carol Danvers' death or corruption.** Singular highest-impact catastrophic input.
- **The reactivation of buried HYDRA programming under conditions where she harms someone in her chosen circle.** This is the nightmare scenario and the one she silently models against in her own operational decisions, whether she would admit it or not.

---

### 9.8 Summary Judgment

The subject is, for the first time in her published existence, **walking a path of her own choosing on terrain she partly controls**. The progress is real and is the product of decades of accumulated, costly adaptation. It is also fragile in specific, identifiable ways, and the entities most likely to test that fragility are still in the field. The forward assessment is **cautiously optimistic on a five-year horizon, materially uncertain on a ten-year horizon, and structurally dependent on the integrity of her chosen-family network and on her continued willingness to permit help on the days when permitting help is hardest**.

She has built something. Whether she keeps it is the open question of the rest of her life.
